She does not maintain a fixed address in the canonical record; her apartment situation is intermittent, and observed sleeping locations have included Sotomayor housing (in flashback), Kate's couch, Avengers facilities used as crash space, and — surveillance-relevant — locations *off-Earth* and *off-timeline* where she appears to have constructed informal lodgings.

### 4.3 Catalina (2021–present)

The single most behaviorally consequential development in the recent record is the existence and accessibility of the biological sister. Catalina functions in the subject's life as a *forced practice ground* for the relational skills the rest of her psychology was built to avoid. Observed patterns:

- Visits to Washington Heights are now regular rather than ceremonial. Subject has been seen at the same bodega across multiple appearances — a *route* has formed, which for a subject whose self-concept is built on route-refusal is a structural change.
- Conversations with Catalina trigger the subject's restlessness-tells (foot-tapping, hand-flexing, the small involuntary glance upward consistent with portal-readiness) but the subject *stays in the chair.* This is a new behavior. It is the first sustained evidence in canon of the subject tolerating an affective state without kinetic discharge.
- Catalina is the only person who knows the Edge League material from the inside. She is, therefore, the only person to whom the subject does not have to *explain* — which is the precondition under which the subject can tolerate proximity to her own history.

There is no evidence the subject has discussed Catalina at any depth with Kate Bishop. The compartmentalization between her closest peer relationship and her closest blood relationship is total. This is consistent with her established pattern of running parallel, non-intersecting attachment tracks — a deactivation strategy that prevents any single relational rupture from collapsing the whole system.

### 4.4 The Romantic Field (post-Halloran)

The Lisa Halloran relationship remains the only sustained on-page romantic partnership in the subject's record, and its dissolution remains uninterrogated in any depicted therapeutic or introspective frame. In the post-2021 window:

- No new sustained partnership has been logged on-panel.
- Casual/short-duration encounters are implied but not foregrounded; the subject's sexual identity remains stable, untroubled, and not a domain of conflict.
- The subject's avoidance of sustained romantic intimacy *outlasts* the integration progress made on the family-of-origin axis. This is diagnostically important: the early-childhood loss is being addressed (via Catalina), but the *relational template that loss installed* — exit before being exited on — is still governing partnership behavior. Integration is occurring in patches, not as a unified front.

UATU assessment: a romantic partnership of any depth in the next operational window would constitute a higher-order stressor than the *Made in the USA* revisions did, because it would require the subject to tolerate someone who is neither family-by-blood (Catalina, can't-be-left) nor friend-by-acceptance (Kate, demands nothing) but rather an active claimant on her presence. There is no canonical evidence she is yet capable of sustaining such a configuration. There is also no evidence she has stopped wanting it.

### 4.5 The Multiversal-Crisis Tempo (2022–2024)

The subject's operational environment in this window has been defined by sustained multiversal instability — *incursions*, breached reality membranes, the cascade-class events that have dominated the larger publication landscape. For most powered subjects this would constitute novel stress. For this subject it is *the medium in which her power is most natural and her affect is most regulated.* Walking between realities is her baseline mode; a publication era in which the membrane between realities is unstable is, paradoxically, a *low-affect* period for her. She is observed in this window as *calmer in crisis than in domesticity* — which is a textbook trauma-adapted operator profile.

Tactical observations from the crisis tempo:

- Portal economy. She has become more efficient with the star-portal capacity — fewer, larger, more strategically placed. Where the early record shows portal-creation used as punctuation (a way to end a conversation, a way to discharge), the recent record shows it used as *infrastructure* (extraction routes for non-flyers, scaffolded retreats, time-arbitraged flanking). This is the maturation of a capability from affect-regulation tool into tactical instrument. The affect-regulation function has not disappeared; it has been *supplemented* by genuine tactical sophistication.
- Threat-reading remains the sharp end. Her early-detection of bad-faith actors (the diagnostic Loki precedent) holds across the recent record; she has flagged at least one infiltrator-class threat to a team before the team itself registered the anomaly.
- Combat damage tolerance unchanged. She still does not present for care, still does not show convalescence on-panel, still re-enters action faster than the rest of the field. The somatic identity ("I do not get hurt") is intact and load-bearing.

### 4.6 Public Profile and Cultural Footprint

The subject's public visibility has expanded considerably outside her direct control. The 2022 cinematic appearance (a recast / modernized origin for screen) introduced her to a global audience an order of magnitude larger than the comics readership, and the canonical subject's reaction to this — to the extent in-universe analogs are observable — has been characteristic: she ignores it. She does not perform celebrity, does not appear to engage with media of herself, does not capitalize on the profile for resource extraction. This is consistent with her established indifference to status hierarchies and her preference for verdict-by-action over reputation-by-narrative.

Surveillance-relevant secondary effects:

- Increased attention from civilian populations in New York; her star-shaped portal signature is now recognizable to bystanders, which has begun to compromise her operational anonymity in a way she does not appear to have adapted to.
- Increased attention from hostile parties seeking multiversal-traversal capability. This is the highest-trending threat vector in the recent window. The subject is the most accessible walking instance of a working interdimensional traversal capacity on Earth-616, and her solo operational posture makes her a target for capture-class adversaries who want the capability rather than her death. She has not, as of the most recent observation, been successfully captured. The pattern suggests she has begun, perhaps without articulating it, to vary her transit signatures and travel routes — early evidence of operational counter-surveillance discipline that did not characterize her earlier years.

### 4.7 Madrimar and the Utopian Parallel Question

The grandmother (Madrimar) and the Utopian Parallel as a place — the elements introduced in the Rivera run that were retconned into a *partial* confabulation by *Made in the USA* — remain unresolved in the current record. The subject has not made a depicted return visit to the Parallel in the recent window. Whether this is avoidance, scheduling, or unspoken disillusionment with the revised origin is not directly attested. UATU inference: it is avoidance. The subject is metabolizing the Washington Heights material; she does not have the bandwidth to also re-examine the Utopian Parallel material, and her established pattern is to handle one destabilization at a time, in sequence, with action between each.

Madrimar's status (alive, where, accessible) is in operational limbo from the subject's perspective. We log this as an *open file* — a pressure point not currently being pressed, but available to any adversary or ally who chose to press it.

### 4.8 Internal State — Best Inference, Present Day

Synthesizing the behavioral telemetry across the recent window:

The subject is in the most psychologically integrated phase of her published life, *and is still substantially un-integrated.* The progress is real and measurable: a route to Washington Heights now exists, a sister now exists, the worst origin-secret is now consciously held, and the kinetic-discharge frequency has dropped. The unfinished work is also real and measurable: the romantic-attachment template is unrevised, the Utopian Parallel question is shelved rather than answered, the grief for the Madres is no more processed than it was a decade ago — only re-contextualized, and that incompletely. The introspective vocabulary remains thin. She still does not present for care.

Affect baseline: stable, dysphoric-irritable under stillness, animated-warm in motion and in the company of Kate or Catalina. No depressive features. No anxiety features classically expressed. No psychotic, manic, or substance-related concerns. Mood and identity functioning are within her established personal baseline, which is the only baseline against which she should be measured.

Operational posture: solo-default, team-available, multiverse-mobile, New-York-anchored for the first time in her adult life. She maintains the exits — the portals are always one kick away — but she is, for the moment, choosing not to use them as often. The choice is the development. The capacity to leave is what makes the choice to stay legible.

### 4.9 Current Location and Status

Most recent observed position: Earth-616, primarily New York metropolitan area, with regular transits to (a) the West Coast for Kate Bishop, (b) Washington Heights for Catalina, (c) various off-world and cross-temporal points for ongoing mission tempo. No fixed legal address. No documented employment. No documented institutional affiliation in any binding sense. Civil identity intact, public name and operating name identical (a refusal of separation between civilian and powered selves that is itself a behavioral datum — she does not split herself into roles).

Health: presumed excellent, untested by any care provider in the depicted record.
Threat to others: low, modulated by her moral spine.
Threat to self: low.
Risk of disappearance from the observable record: moderate-to-high — she retains, by power and by temperament, the capacity to step out of any observer's frame at will. That she has not done so recently is the most important development logged in this section.

**File status: open. Continuing observation recommended.**


## Medical History

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION 2: MEDICAL HISTORY

## Subject: America Chavez

---

## 2.1 Constitutional Baseline

The subject presents as a phenotypically female human of Latina (Puerto Rican / Dominican-coded, per Washington Heights origin) descent, apparent biological age in the early-to-mid twenties across the contemporary record, with somatic markers stable from her first appearance in 2011 onward — a flat developmental curve consistent either with the "Utopian Parallel" aging anomaly the subject herself endorses, or with the engineered-physiology hypothesis advanced in *Made in the USA*. Recorded height fluctuates by artist (approximately 5'8"–5'10"), build mesomorphic-athletic with documented hypertrophy of the gluteal, quadriceps, and gastrocnemius groups disproportionate to the upper body — a fact of biomechanical signature, not aesthetic: this is a body organized around the legs because the legs are the weapon and the vehicle.

Resting somatic affect is *kinetic-ready*. The subject does not stand at parade rest; she stands weight-shifted, knees soft, one foot slightly forward, hands loose — the posture of someone who expects to leave in any direction without warning. In medical-surveillance terms: the autonomic baseline is permanently tilted toward sympathetic activation, but stably so. She is not anxious; she is *cocked*.

Vital signs, where inferable from depicted exertion-to-recovery curves, suggest cardiovascular capacity orders of magnitude beyond human norm — no observable winding after extended atmospheric flight, multi-reality combat sequences, or sustained ground-pounding. No depicted sweating beyond cosmetic. No depicted shivering, even in vacuum or in the cold gradients of inter-reality transit.

---

## 2.2 The Engineered Substrate (Pediatric Medical Trauma)

Per the *America Chavez: Made in the USA* (2021) record, the subject's powers were not constitutional to a Utopian biology but were the product of pediatric experimental procedures conducted on her and her younger sister Catalina in Washington Heights — the so-called Santana procedure under the auspices of the "Edge League." This places, at the substrate of every subsequent medical and psychological observation, a foundational fact: **the subject's body is the site of childhood non-consensual medical experimentation.** The powers — strength, flight, near-invulnerability, dimensional portal generation — are scar tissue. They are also, functionally, prosthetics: capacities grafted onto a pediatric nervous system that did not request them and could not consent.

The clinical sequelae of this are present whether or not the subject acknowledges them:

- **Aversion to clinical settings.** Across the entire published record, the subject is never depicted seeking medical care. Not once. Injuries that on any human would constitute hospital admissions are walked off. This is not bravado alone; it is a documented avoidance pattern wholly consistent with childhood medical trauma — the examination table is the original site of harm, and adult bodies that bear childhood medical trauma reliably refuse adult medical contact.
- **Somatic dissociation from pain-reporting.** The subject does not narrate her injuries. She does not say "that hurt." When asked, she deflects to mission status. The *Made in the USA* memory-rewriting hypothesis — that her foundational story was psychologically reconstructed to shield her from the abuse memory — extends naturally to the body: she does not report pain because reporting pain was, in childhood, the precondition for further procedure.
- **Tolerance for invasive sensation.** Portal-generation involves, by inference, the subject's leg passing through the membrane between realities — a sensation that is never depicted as pleasurable or comfortable, only as functional. She has normalized an invasive somatic experience as a tool, which is consistent with a childhood in which invasive somatic experience was normalized as routine.
- **The sister.** Catalina's existence — discovered in *Made in the USA* — is itself a medical fact: a co-survivor of the same procedure, a person whose body confirms what the subject's body has been rewritten not to remember. The subject's response to Catalina is the most somatically destabilized she is ever depicted being. The body recognizes what the narrative cannot.

---

## 2.3 Power-Set Inventory and Biomechanical Notes

### 2.3.1 Superhuman Strength

Top-tier within the powered population — sustained engagement with Asgardian and Kree-class opponents without measurable degradation. Strength is generalized (not limited to legs) but the *application* signature is leg-dominant: kicks, knees, ground-pound impacts, and braced full-body pushes. Upper-body strikes are present but secondary; the subject does not box. She kicks. She tackles. She portals.

Clinically: the musculoskeletal loading on her own skeleton during these feats would, on a baseline human chassis, produce catastrophic injury. That it does not implies either skeletal reinforcement at the cellular level (densified osseous matrix) or a field effect that distributes impact across the body. There is no depicted scan or workup confirming which.

### 2.3.2 Flight

Self-propelled, atmospheric and exo-atmospheric, with no observable propulsion mechanism — i.e. she is not jet-propelled, not gravity-manipulating in any depicted way, simply *flying*. Speed sub-orbital at minimum, interstellar in *Ultimates* contexts. No depicted vertigo, no depicted G-LOC, no depicted vacuum stress. This is the second mobility system — the redundancy is telling. Even when grounded, she can leave. Even when she cannot portal, she can fly. The body is built around exit options.

### 2.3.3 Near-Invulnerability

No catalogued scar tissue. No depicted permanent disfigurement. Conventional ordnance is non-issue; energy weapons produce transient effects; only meta-class force (Mother, the Demiurge-tier Loki manifestations, cosmic-tier impacts) registers as injury. The clinical concern here is not the toughness itself but the *consequence* of it: the subject has lived a life in which her body has never failed her in any visible way, which means she has no embodied experience of fragility, which means she has no embodied training in the affect-management skills that fragility teaches.

In plain terms: she does not know what it feels like to be weak. This is a medical fact with psychological weight.

### 2.3.4 Star-Portal Generation

The signature capacity. Five-pointed apertures kicked through the substrate of reality, traversing dimensions, timelines, parallel universes, and pocket realities. Biomechanically, this is the most diagnostically interesting power in the inventory: it is *somatic*, *leg-executed*, *kinetic-initiated*. It is not gestured. It is not willed in stillness. It requires the body to move.

Implications:
- The subject cannot leave a room by thought. She must use her body to leave. This couples mobility to embodiment in a way that makes stillness somatically intolerable.
- The portal is generated by *striking* — the act of leaving is the act of impact. Departure and aggression are neurologically fused. To go is to hit.
- Per *Made in the USA*, the portal capacity is not fully understood by the subject herself; she has on occasion overdrawn it (mis-targeted portals, drained capacity after extended use), suggesting it operates on a resource pool she does not consciously monitor. She does not know her own limits because she has never been incentivized to learn them.

### 2.3.5 Undocumented / Variable Capacities

Across writers, intermittent feats appear and disappear: low-level energy emission (the "star-bolts" of certain depictions), temporary durability extensions under emotional load, brief telepathic-adjacent recognition of multiversal anomalies. These are not stable enough to chart as confirmed capacities; they are noted here for completeness as potential capability surges under affective stress — a pattern that, if confirmed, would suggest the power-set is partially modulated by emotional state, which would have downstream implications for any scenario in which the subject is emotionally compromised in a high-stakes operational context.

---

## 2.4 Injury Log (Reconstructed)

Because the subject does not present for care and does not convalesce on-panel, the injury record must be reconstructed from depicted combat damage and inferred recovery. Patterns:

- ***Vengeance* (2011) era:** Multiple high-impact engagements with In-Betweener forces. No depicted recovery. Walk-off baseline established.
- ***Young Avengers* (2013):** Trans-dimensional combat against Mother and the Mother-parasites; extended exposure to non-Euclidean physics; direct combat with multiple Loki manifestations including the demiurgic adult form. Injuries shown as bruising and ablated costume; no depicted convalescence. Notable: the subject sustains a significant blow in the final battle and is upright within the same scene.
- ***America* (2017) #4–6:** Combat damage from Exterminatrix and the Midas Corporation goons; facial bruising present in subsequent panels but no medical attention sought; bruising fades across two issues without narrative comment. The subject re-enters the field while still visibly injured — a pattern of *injury-tolerance-as-identity-confirmation* (the body proves the self by refusing to acknowledge harm).
- ***Made in the USA* (2021):** Direct confrontation with the architects of the Santana procedure; sustained physical injury *and*, more significantly, the first depicted **neurological / dissociative injury** — destabilization of the memory-confabulation produces brief fugue-adjacent episodes, the closest the subject comes to a documented decompensation. This is the only "injury" in the entire record that she cannot walk off, and it is not a physical injury at all.
- ***Ultimates* (Ewing) era:** Cosmic-tier engagements, including direct exposure to Galactus-class energies and chronal-distortion fields; no depicted injury sequelae. Notable for the absence of any temporal-physiological effect — the subject's body appears to be resistant to chronal manipulation, possibly an artifact of multiverse-native physiology, possibly an engineered durability against the very forces her portal-power exposes her to.
- ***West Coast Avengers* (Thompson):** Lower-stakes street and B-list-cosmic engagements; no notable injuries. Notable instead for the subject's depicted comfort in this register — lower threat means lower somatic activation, and she is depicted *more relaxed in posture* in these issues than in any other era of the record.

The aggregate injury record is unusual not for its severity but for its *narrative invisibility*. A surveillance file on a baseline-human operator of comparable combat exposure would run hundreds of pages of trauma center admissions, physical therapy intakes, and recovery diaries. The subject's file is blank in that column. This is not absence of injury; it is absence of *injury-acknowledgment behavior*.

---

## 2.5 Substances, Sleep, Sex, Appetite

**Substances.** Social alcohol use depicted in college-era and team-social contexts (*America* solo, post-mission gatherings in *West Coast Avengers*). No depicted intoxication beyond mild. No tobacco. No cannabis. No depicted recreational pharmaceuticals. No depicted caffeine dependency — though it would be diagnostically interesting if she did rely on caffeine, given her baseline activation. The absence of any substance-management behavior suggests the subject regulates affect without chemical assistance because her primary regulator (kinetic discharge) is always available; she does not need a drink because she can punch through a wall.

**Sleep.** Rarely depicted. When depicted, brief — the subject is shown awake at unusual hours across multiple runs, often departing for solo missions while others sleep. No depicted nightmare sequences (notable, given the trauma history — consistent with the §3 finding that the intrusion channel is suppressed). No depicted insomnia complaints, but a pattern of *under-sleeping by preference* is detectable. Stillness, even the stillness of sleep, is something she takes in minimum doses.

**Sex.** Canonically lesbian, identity stable, no depicted internal conflict. Sexual functioning within normal limits where depicted (the Lisa Halloran relationship in *America* is depicted as sexually active and affectively warm during its functional phase). The relational *exit pattern* is psychological, not somatic — the body shows up; the attachment system does not stay. Note for completeness: the subject's choice of partners across the record skews toward women who do not demand processing — Lisa was the exception, and the relationship dissolved.

**Appetite.** Robust, depicted enthusiastically — burgers, diner food, street food, the Latin-coded cuisine of her Washington Heights / Sotomayor environment. No depicted disordered eating. Appetite is one of the unambiguously pleasurable somatic domains in her record. She eats with the same posture she fights with: forward, committed, taking up space.

---

## 2.6 Surgical / Procedural History

No adult surgical history depicted. The only procedural history in the record is the pediatric Santana procedure itself (per *Made in the USA*) — the foundational, non-consensual, identity-engineering intervention that produced the powered phenotype. It is, in the strictest sense, the *only* procedure she has ever had, and it is the one she does not remember having had. The medical file is, in this sense, a single line item written in childhood and suppressed from conscious access for two decades.

The clinical consequence: any future medical contact — even benign, even welcome — will be processed by her nervous system through the schema of that original procedure. A blood draw is not a blood draw to this subject. A scan is not a scan. This is the relevant fact for any clinician who ever attempts contact, and the relevant fact for any adversary who ever attempts to immobilize her in a clinical-adjacent setting (restraints, examination, sedation): the response will be disproportionate to the proximate stimulus because the proximate stimulus is not what is being responded to.

---

## 2.7 Transformations and Reality-State Alterations

The subject has been subjected to several reality-altering events that warrant inclusion in the medical record because they constitute *somatic events*, even where the somatic medium is metaphysical:

- **Mother's reality-collapse exposure (*Young Avengers*):** Extended exposure to a reality-eating parasitic entity. No depicted residual effect on the subject specifically, though teammates show varying sequelae. The subject's apparent immunity is consistent with multiverse-native physiology.
- **Loki's manipulations:** Repeated exposure to reality-distortion fields. The subject demonstrated unusual resistance — she alone perceived the manipulation early. Whether this is a *perceptual* power-feature or a *characterological* feature (paranoid baseline producing accurate threat-detection in a high-deception environment) is not adjudicable from the record. Likely both.
- **Utopian Parallel revelations (*America* solo):** Discovery that the constructed origin was partially a narrative imposition. This produced what is best described as a *cognitive-somatic* injury — brief dissociation, posture-shift to defensive crouch, and immediate kinetic exit. The body registered the destabilization before the mind did.
- ***Made in the USA* revelations:** The most severe of these events — the comprehensive collapse of the originating narrative and exposure to the actual childhood medical trauma. Somatic signs included tremor, breath-control failure, and brief dissociative fugue. The subject re-stabilized through action (re-engagement with the antagonists, re-assertion of operational identity), but this is the documented high-water mark for decompensation in the record and the closest the subject has come to a true clinical event.
- **Cosmic-tier energy exposures (*Ultimates*):** Galactus-adjacent exposures, chronal-field traversal, multiversal incursion engagements. No depicted somatic sequelae. The subject appears to be among the most cosmically-durable operators in the published roster, a fact that has not been clinically explained.

---

## 2.8 Disabilities

None depicted in the physical register. The relevant disabilities are functional and psychological, addressed in §3, but two warrant flagging here as having somatic substrate:

1. **Stillness intolerance.** Not a recognized clinical disability but a documented functional impairment. The subject cannot remain still without somatic distress. In lecture halls (*America*), in convalescence (absent), in any imposed stasis, the body initiates micro-movement: toe-tap, jaw-clench, postural shift, eventual exit. If forcibly immobilized for clinically significant durations, the prediction is rapid somatic-affective decompensation. This is a real, mappable, somatic limit.

2. **Interoceptive deficit.** The subject does not appear to read her own internal states accurately. Pain, fatigue, hunger when emotionally activated, and emotional signals generally are under-reported and under-noticed. This is consistent with the trauma history (chronically dissociated bodies become chronically illiterate bodies) and has the operational consequence that she will routinely under-estimate her own resource depletion. She will not know she is exhausted until she falls down, and she will not fall down until far past the point a self-attuned body would have rested.

---

## 2.9 Synthesis

The medical file on this subject is, in the conventional sense, almost empty: no surgeries, no chronic conditions, no medication list, no admissions, no scars. In the *meaningful* sense, it is one of the densest files in the powered population — because what is absent from the file is itself the diagnosis. The subject does not present for care because she was, in childhood, the subject of care that harmed her. The subject does not narrate pain because pain-narration was, in childhood, the gateway to further harm. The subject's body is built for exit because the body's first experience was of being held in place against its will. The powers themselves — the strength that never fails, the flight that needs no ground, the portals kicked through reality with the legs that were once strapped to a table — are the somatic memorial to the original procedure, dressed up as the costume of a hero.

She is, medically speaking, the healthiest patient who has never seen a doctor. She is also, medically speaking, an emergency waiting for the one stimulus her defenses are not built for: a clinician kind enough, and patient enough, to ask her to sit still and tell them where it hurts.


## Somatic Atlas

# SOMATIC ATLAS: AMERICA CHAVEZ

*Compiled longitudinally from observational record, 2011–present. This section maps the body as the primary instrument of the subject's psychology — given that affect regulation in this case is overwhelmingly kinetic, the body is also the most reliable diagnostic surface.*

---

## 1. BASELINE MORPHOLOGY AND POSTURAL SIGNATURE

The subject stands roughly 5'8", densely muscled in a manner that reads less "athletic-trained" than "developmentally heavy" — the muscle mass is the substrate of her engineered physiology rather than the product of a gym regimen, and she carries it as if it were her ordinary weight, never bracing against it. Shoulders ride high and slightly forward; clavicles broad and squared. The trapezius is permanently engaged, even at rest — palpation would find no slack in the upper back. This is not consciously held tension; it is structural baseline. The standing posture is *grounded forward*: weight distributed approximately 60/40 onto the balls of the feet, knees never fully locked, hips squared but slightly tilted into a readiness stance. She does not stand the way civilians stand. She *stages* on a floor.

Hands at rest are rarely actually at rest. The default is a loose fist with the thumb riding over the index knuckle — a fighter's idle, not a clenched fist of anger but a hand always halfway to function. When she does open her hands (in repose, in conversation with Kate Bishop, in moments with the Madres in retrospect-panels), the fingers splay wider than necessary, as if she has to consciously contradict the closure.

The chin carries slightly elevated — three to five degrees above neutral — producing the persistent impression of looking *down at* whatever she is looking at, regardless of relative height. This calibrates dynamically: with peers and children it disappears; with authority figures, antagonists, and any speaker of an opinion she finds soft, it sharpens.

---

## 2. GAIT AND LOCOMOTION

The walking gait is heel-strong, slightly wider-than-hip-width track, with a measurable lateral roll at the pelvis that produces what observers in-universe and out have characterized as a "swagger." The mechanics are real: hip rotation runs roughly 8–12 degrees greater than population baseline, arm swing is reduced (the arms are kept available for use rather than counterbalance), and the stride length is approximately 5–10% longer than her leg length would predict — she is always traveling slightly faster than the apparent pace.

The walk has three diagnostic variants:

- **The corridor walk** (transit through a place she does not own — campus halls, team headquarters she did not pick): faster, hips more level, arms slightly more swung, eyes tracking exits. Resembles a civilian's brisk walk except that her shoulders never round forward.
- **The arrival walk** (entering a room she intends to dominate, including most combat ingress): slower than the corridor walk, deeper hip roll, chin a degree higher, hand-fists looser. The cadence here is musical — beat-driven, suggesting an internal rhythm she is walking *to*.
- **The departure walk** (leaving a conversation she has decided is finished): nearly identical to the arrival walk but with the head angled slightly away from the person she is leaving. She does not look back. The absence of the look-back is one of the most reliable behavioral markers in the file.

Running is rare — she flies or portals — but when observed (typically when she is conserving cosmic effort or operating in a no-fly civil environment), the run is heavy-footed, full-strike, no toe-running, and she does not pace herself. She runs at one speed: maximum-sustainable.

Flight posture is upright more often than horizontal, which is unusual among flying capes; she hovers and travels feet-down, arms slightly out from the body, as if walking on an unseen floor. The horizontal flight posture appears only at high speeds or during combat ingress. This is a tell: she prefers to remain *vertical* in space — to keep the relationship between her body and a ground she would land on. It is a controlled-fall person's preference.

---

## 3. THE PORTAL KICK AND COMBAT MICRO-MECHANICS

The signature portal-creating action — the star-kick — is biomechanically a near-perfect roundhouse from the right leg approximately 70% of the time, an axe-kick approximately 20%, and a stomp from a stationary stance approximately 10%. The left-leg portal exists but is markedly less smooth; she has a clear dominant kicking leg. Before the kick, there is a quarter-second tell: the standing-leg knee bends roughly 5 degrees deeper than necessary for the kick alone, loading. Adversaries who survive long enough to learn it (almost none) could read the load.

Pre-combat, the body runs through a brief unconscious checklist: a roll of the right shoulder, a flex-and-release of both hands, a single hard exhale through the nose, and a fractional lowering of the chin from its baseline elevation. This is invariant across nearly every documented engagement. It takes approximately 1.2 seconds. She does not appear to know she does it.

Strike preference is closed-fist, lead with the right hook. The hook is thrown from the hip, not the shoulder — she punches like a brawler, not a boxer. Against opponents she respects, the form tightens and the lead changes; against ones she does not, she leans into the brawl. Loki, in *Young Avengers*, got the brawl form.

She does not block. She steps off-line or absorbs. The absence of blocking-as-habit is itself diagnostic — her invulnerability has trained out the defensive reflex civilians and most fighters retain. The cost is that she has no muscle-memory for protecting another person's body from incoming force; she will instead interpose her *whole body*, which she does reliably and without hesitation.

---

## 4. FACIAL PATTERN AND MICRO-EXPRESSION

The face at rest is set in what a clinician would call a *resting confident face* — the corners of the mouth held a millimeter or two above neutral, the brow slightly down, the eyes wide and steady. It is not a smile and not a scowl. It is a face prepared to be looked at without flinching.

The smile, when it arrives, is large and asymmetric — pulls higher on the right side, shows upper teeth, often accompanied by a slight head-tilt to the left. Genuine smiles reach the orbital muscles and crinkle the outer eyes; performed smiles (offered to people she is managing rather than enjoying) stop at the cheek. The differential is reliable.

The laugh is loud, throat-open, head-back — a brief and total commitment to mirth, after which the face returns to baseline with no transitional softening. She does not chuckle. She either laughs entirely or does not.

Micro-expression tells:

- **The jaw set.** When she is about to disagree, the masseter clenches once — visible as a small lateral movement at the angle of the jaw — before she speaks. Reliable predictor of incoming "no."
- **The single eyebrow raise** (right side preferred). Functions as her primary skepticism marker; replaces a verbal "really?" approximately half the time.
- **The lip-corner pull** (downward, unilateral, right side). Disgust or contempt. Brief — under 200 milliseconds. Reserved for cruelty witnessed, bigotry, and certain authority figures.
- **The nostril flare on inhale.** Anger marker. When this appears, kinetic discharge follows within approximately 30 seconds unless interrupted by a trusted voice (Kate's voice has been documented to interrupt it; few others).
- **The slow blink.** Rare. Appears when she is being told something that contradicts a foundational narrative — observed in *Made in the USA* during the Catalina sequences. Should be coded as the highest-grade distress signal her face produces. She does not weep; she slow-blinks.

Eye contact is hard, sustained, and slightly *over*-held by population norms — she will out-stare almost any interlocutor, and breaking eye contact is a deliberate gift. With children and with Kate, the eye contact softens and becomes intermittent in a normative range. With Lisa Halloran, late in the relationship, the eye contact began to skip — a clean somatic readout of the avoidant withdrawal that preceded her verbal departure.

Tears: documented on perhaps five occasions across the entire record. They arrive without facial collapse — the rest of the face stays composed and the tears simply emerge, are not wiped, and are not commented on. She does not cry into anyone. She cries while continuing to look forward.

---

## 5. VOCAL AND SPEECH SOMATICS

The voice sits in the lower-middle alto range, with a chest-resonant placement that carries without effort. Volume baseline is approximately 10–15% louder than civilian conversational norms; she does not modulate down in quiet spaces unless reminded, and even then drifts back up within a minute or two.

Cadence is declarative — falling intonation at the end of nearly every sentence, including questions. The interrogative uplift is largely absent from her speech, which produces the characteristic impression that even her questions are statements awaiting confirmation. Sentence length is short; subordinate clauses are rare. The grammar is verb-forward.

Code-switching into Spanish is state-dependent and is one of the most reliable affect markers in the file:

- **Calm / baseline:** occasional lexical insertions ("princesa," "nena"), mostly affectionate, often directed at Kate or at children.
- **Heightened affect (anger, grief, love):** whole phrases, often imperatives or invocations ("ya basta," "mi amor," invocations of the Madres). The Spanish carries the emotion the English declines to.
- **Foundational destabilization:** the language ratio inverts; English becomes the second language and the Spanish carries the narrative. Observed in the most intimate scenes with her grandmother and during the *Made in the USA* recovery sequences.

Verbal tics include: "girl" as a punctuation mark, sentence-initial "look —", and the rhetorical "you serious?" deployed when something has surprised or offended her. Profanity is moderate, not florid, used for emphasis rather than texture.

She does not fill silences. When uncertain, she goes quiet rather than verbal; the quiet is hard and uncomfortable for interlocutors, which is part of its function. Pauses can run to ten seconds before she chooses whether to speak or to leave.

Breath is a tell. The single hard nasal exhale precedes combat (see §3) but also precedes any decision to *exit* a conversation — same exhale, different downstream behavior. The breath itself is the decision-point; whatever follows the exhale is the chosen action.

---

## 6. HANDS, GESTURE, AND OBJECT-HANDLING

Gestures are large, planar, and arm-driven — she gestures from the shoulder, not from the wrist. The dominant gesture is an open-palmed lateral sweep that functions as a verbal *no*, *stop*, or *enough*. Point-gestures are emphatic and use the whole hand (chopping motion) rather than an isolated index finger; the isolated index finger appears only when she is genuinely accusing someone.

She touches objects more heavily than necessary. Doors are pushed open with full-body commitment (and frequently broken — observed multiple times across the record, played for comedy but consistent enough to be a baseline calibration problem). Cups are gripped firmly; phones are held tight. She has not been observed to handle anything delicate without conscious effort. Fine motor work is competent but not preferred; her hands are calibrated to a different scale of object.

She does not fidget in the classical sense — no pen-clicking, no foot-jiggling, no nail-picking. The restlessness manifests at the *gross* level: she gets up, she paces, she leaves. The body refuses small repetitive discharge and demands large discharge.

Touch with others is selective. Initiated touch is rare and meaningful — a hand on a shoulder, a forearm clasp, an arm slung across Kate's shoulders. She does not hug spontaneously; hugs initiated by others are received with a slight delay (approximately half a second of stillness before her arms close) and ended by her, not the other party. The hug-ending is consistent: a single firm pat on the back, then release.

---

## 7. GROOMING, DRESS, AND PRESENTATION

The hair is worn long, dark, and unfussy — typically loose, sometimes pulled back for combat with a single elastic. She does not visibly style. The hair is washed and present and not negotiated with further.

Eye makeup is consistently present in non-combat depictions — winged liner, sometimes a defined brow. It is the one element of her presentation that is *crafted* rather than functional, and it is consistent enough across writers and artists to register as a true personal habit rather than artistic convention. It is also the only domain where she practices a daily ritual of *stillness* in front of a mirror, which is psychologically notable.

Wardrobe is fixed in palette: red, white, blue, with a denim jacket as near-uniform off-duty. The star motif recurs across nearly every outfit she chooses. Shorts and boots are the lower-body default; she does not wear restrictive clothing and does not appear to own anything that limits range of motion at the hip. Footwear is heavy — boots with substantial soles, laced tight. She kicks reality through her feet; the feet are dressed accordingly.

She does not wear jewelry of consequence. No watch (she has internalized time elsewhere). No rings. Earrings occasionally — small studs, never dangling.

She is observed showering and dressing only in brief panels but the rhythm is fast and efficient; she does not linger in front of mirrors except for the eye makeup. There is no documented evidence of mirror-checking behavior, body-scrutiny, or grooming anxiety. The body is an instrument she maintains, not a surface she audits.

---

## 8. SLEEP ARCHITECTURE

Sleep is documented only sparingly. The available record indicates: short total sleep duration (estimated 5–6 hours), late sleep onset, early waking, and a notable absence of any depicted nightmare sequence — diagnostically significant for a subject with this trauma load. The classical PTSD nightmare channel does not appear to be active; trauma is metabolized through daytime kinesis, not nocturnal intrusion.

Sleep posture, where observed, is on the back or stomach, arms above the head or under the pillow — never the curled fetal side-sleep. She does not coil for sleep. The body remains open and ready even unconscious.

She does not appear to sleep in the same place twice for long stretches. Across the published record she has slept in: a dorm at Sotomayor, various team facilities, the Utopian Parallel, multiple pocket dimensions, a borrowed couch in Washington Heights. The portable sleep capacity is itself a tell — she does not anchor to a bed. Insomnia, where it appears, is not turned into rumination but into transit: she gets up, she goes somewhere.

There is no documented bedtime ritual. No reading, no music, no wind-down. She is awake and then she is asleep; she is asleep and then she is up.

---

## 9. EATING AND INGESTION

Appetite is large and untroubled. She eats fast, finishes plates, prefers dense and savory food, and gravitates toward food coded to her cultural origin (Dominican and Puerto Rican dishes in the Washington Heights material) and to portable street food in transit contexts. She does not appear to have food aversions, dietary restrictions, or eating-disordered patterns of any kind. The eating domain is uncomplicated.

She eats with her hands more readily than with utensils where culturally appropriate. She chews loudly enough to be observed. She does not perform delicacy at the table.

Hydration appears casual. She drinks water when thirsty, alcohol socially (beer and rum-based cocktails in observation), coffee functionally and without ceremony. She has been depicted drunk perhaps twice — both times loose and warm rather than aggressive, leaning into Kate, more verbally affectionate than baseline. Alcohol disinhibits toward intimacy, not toward conflict. This is a benign and stable signature.

No tobacco. No documented drug use. The body is treated as an asset, not a punishment surface.

---

## 10. SEXUAL AND INTIMATE SOMATICS

Sexuality is one of the unconflicted domains. The body in sexual contexts moves with the same confident commitment it brings to combat — she initiates, she leads, she does not perform smallness. With Lisa Halloran, in the panels depicting the relationship at its closest, the body is responsive and warm; the disengagement that ended the relationship was not somatic-sexual but post-coital and affective, the inability to *stay* in the proximity that followed the act.

Touch in intimacy is firm rather than feather-light; she does not hover. She kisses with full mouth contact and closed eyes — the eyes-closed kiss is notable given her general preference for visual control, and may be the single domain where she relinquishes scanning behavior. Post-intimacy, the body does not stay coiled around the partner; she will hold for a measured period (estimated several minutes) and then disengage to lie adjacent rather than entwined. This is the somatic version of the Stage 2 pattern from §3 of the workup — physical disengagement precedes the cognitive decision to leave.

Sexual frequency, partners outside the documented record, and contraceptive practice are not in the file. The presentation is of a sexually mature, comfortable, and unburdened adult who is not currently using sexuality as a regulation channel.

---

## 11. STATE-DEPENDENT SOMATIC SHIFTS

Synthesis across the above by state:

- **Calm / with Kate:** chin lowers to neutral, shoulders drop perceptibly, hands open at rest, gesture range narrows, voice volume drops 10–15%, Spanish appears in affectionate insertions, eye contact softens to normative intermittence, the smile reaches the orbital. This is the only configuration in which the upper back has been observed to genuinely relax.
- **In a lecture or required stillness:** leg jiggle (one of the few small-motor exceptions), pen-spinning if a pen is available, frequent posture shifts, gaze drift toward windows and exits. Within 20 minutes she is restless; within 40 she has either left or is no longer cognitively present. The somatic restlessness is the trauma defense refusing the stillness — see psychological workup §3.
- **In conversation that approaches an emotional core:** jaw sets, nostril flare appears on inhale, hands close from rest into the loose fist, eye contact intensifies briefly and then breaks decisively. The hard nasal exhale signals the decision point.
- **In combat:** the chin drops *from* its elevated baseline to neutral or slightly below — counterintuitive but consistent; she fights with her head down. Breathing slows and deepens. Facial affect goes flat. The combat face is the least expressive face in her repertoire. There is no taunting smirk; there is a working face.
- **In threat-detection without engagement** (the Loki-detection mode): stillness, full visual fixation on the threat, breath held briefly, hand of dominant side drifting toward kick-loading stance behind the rear leg. She has been observed to track threats with peripheral vision while appearing to face elsewhere — this is real and consistent.
- **In foundational destabilization** (the *Made in the USA* register): the slow blink, the language inversion to Spanish, brief facial slackness, posture loses its forward weight and becomes momentarily symmetrical and almost civilian — and then re-stabilizes hard, often with a single hard exhale and a chosen action. The window of true vulnerability is approximately five to fifteen seconds long.
- **In grief, isolated:** stands still. This is rare and meaningful. The body that refuses stillness in every other context will, in the moments where she has chosen to remember the Madres or to receive a death, hold a single position for extended periods — minutes — without shift. The body knows how to mourn, but only alone, and only by becoming the opposite of itself for a measured interval before resuming motion.

---

## 12. SUMMARY OBSERVATION

The somatic record is the cleanest available readout of this subject because she has organized her psychology *through* the body rather than against it. The body never lies because the body is the language. To read her, watch the chin, the jaw-set, the nasal exhale, the hand at rest, the language ratio, and — most diagnostically — whether her feet are pointed toward the person she is talking to or toward an exit. The feet decide before the mouth does. They have decided every meaningful event in her life.


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION 7: ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS

## Subject: America Chavez / "Miss America"

---

## 7.1 Attachment Classification & Origin

The subject presents a textbook *dismissive-avoidant* attachment organization with a complex-traumatic underlayer — what attachment researchers in the Main/Goldwyn tradition would code as **Ds3 (restricted in feeling, idealizing)** with intermittent **unresolved/disorganized** markers around the maternal loss. The idealization is loud and operationally visible: the Madres are referenced across nearly every solo issue as flawless, mythic, the gold standard of love and sacrifice. The restriction of feeling is equally visible: when asked, in any sustained way, to describe what she *felt* when they died, the subject either (a) substitutes a story about what they *did*, (b) substitutes a moral about what their sacrifice *means*, or (c) physically removes herself from the conversational frame. Affect about the loss has been replaced by narrative about the loss. This is the signature.

The etiology has three identifiable strata:

1. **Pre-loss baseline (Utopian Parallel period, ages 0 to ~6 in the canonical narrative; ages 0 to ~6 in Washington Heights per the *Made in the USA* revision).** Insufficient data to characterize cleanly, but the absence of any depicted "easy" intimacy even in earliest flashbacks — the subject is shown small but already postured, already arms-crossed, already chin-up — suggests the secure base was never wholly secure even before catastrophe.
2. **The Madres' departure.** The foundational injury. Whether read in original-canon (heroic sacrifice for the Utopian Parallel) or revised-canon (death/abandonment in the context of medical-experimental trauma in Washington Heights), the structural fact is identical: the two people who were supposed to stay, *chose to leave*, and the leaving was framed to the child as love. This is the most pathogenic possible configuration — abandonment encoded as devotion — because it forecloses the normal grief work of being angry at the lost objects. To rage at the Madres would be to defile their sacrifice. So the rage has nowhere to go but into the body and out through the wall.
3. **The post-loss caregiving environment.** Per *Made in the USA*, this includes a sister (Catalina) from whom the subject was separated, and a foster/institutional trajectory through the medical program. The subject did not have a single sustained alternative attachment figure during the critical 6–12 window. The grandmother (Madrimar) enters later and is held at the same idealized-mythic distance as the Madres — useful, revered, not metabolized as ordinary caregiver.

The result is a child who learned the following operational rule before she had language for it: **love is something that arrives, performs sacrifice, and leaves; my job is to be worthy of having been loved; my job is never again to be the one waiting.**

---

## 7.2 The Master Template: "Arrive Before You Are Left"

Every significant relationship in the subject's published record is a variation on a single template, which can be stated with surveillance-grade precision:

> *Enter at high velocity on her own terms. Demonstrate competence and loyalty quickly. Refuse the rituals that would deepen mutual knowledge (sustained vulnerable disclosure, dependency, planning a shared future, asking for help). Stay as long as the relationship makes no claim on her interiority. Exit — physically, dimensionally, or affectively — at the first sustained pressure to be known. Return, often warmly, on her terms, after enough time has elapsed that the pressure has dissipated.*

This is observable in every major dyad: Kate Bishop (the most successful application — Kate never pushes), the Young Avengers as a group (joined, exited, rejoined, exited), Lisa Halloran (the relationship that broke because Lisa, reasonably, asked for *more*), the Ultimates (joined for a mission, deprioritized when the mission ended), West Coast Avengers (a tour, not a residency), her sister Catalina (the *hardest* relationship in the record precisely because Catalina's claim on her cannot be exited through a portal — they share a substrate). The template does not vary; only the texture of the exit varies.

---

## 7.3 Bonding: How She Forms Attachment

The subject bonds *fast and shallow*, then slowly thickens the bond in a narrow band that excludes vulnerability. The observable bonding sequence:

- **Threat-co-presence.** First-stage bonding nearly always occurs in combat or crisis. She is comfortable with people she has fought beside before she is comfortable with people she has eaten breakfast beside. The Young Avengers became "her people" through the Mother arc, not through the team dinners. Kate Bishop became sister-equivalent through scrapes, not through the long talks Kate would have welcomed.
- **Competence verification.** She tests new attachments by giving them tasks and watching how they execute. She does not test by disclosing and watching how they respond. People who pass her competence tests are admitted to a working-loyalty tier; people who pass her *moral* tests (defending the vulnerable, refusing the easy compromise) are admitted to a deeper tier.
- **Joke and barb register.** Once admitted, she communicates affection through teasing, declarative compliments fired sideways, and physical proximity (sitting close, shoulder-bumps, the willingness to be in the same room without speaking). She does not communicate affection through stated feeling. "I love you" is a sentence she can produce under crisis stakes but not as a Tuesday-morning utterance.
- **Code-switch as intimacy marker.** Spanish enters her speech when emotional pressure rises *and* she trusts the listener. With strangers she stays in English even when angry. With Kate, with the Madres in flashback, with Catalina, with herself in private monologue — Spanish surfaces. The code-switch is a more reliable measure of intimacy than any verbal disclosure.

What is conspicuously *absent* from her bonding pattern: requests for help, admissions of fear, descriptions of internal state, planning conversations that presume the relationship's future, and any willingness to *be cared for* in convalescence. She will care for others; she will not let others care for her. Asymmetry of care is the structural feature of every relationship she sustains.

---

## 7.4 Distrust: How She Withholds

Distrust is the subject's default; trust is a slowly-issued visa. The distrust operates on multiple tiers:

- **Tier 1 — Authority figures and institutions.** Refused on contact. Adult heroes, mentors, team leaders, university administrators, the medical establishment — all begin in a position of suspicion from which they must climb. The Loki episode in *Young Avengers* is diagnostic: where the rest of the team needed multiple deceptions to register threat, the subject distrusted on principle from the first room.
- **Tier 2 — People who want to know her.** This is the operationally important category. Anyone who asks the second question after "how are you?" — anyone who notices the deflection and tries again — triggers a withdrawal protocol. The withdrawal can be subtle (topic change, joke, physical reorientation away from the speaker) or overt (leaving the room, leaving the planet). Lisa Halloran is the clearest case: a girlfriend whose entirely reasonable desire to be let in was experienced by the subject as a slow encirclement.
- **Tier 3 — People who tell her about herself.** Anyone who offers an interpretation of her behavior, her history, or her affect is met with hard refusal — not argument, *refusal*. She does not debate diagnoses of herself. She vacates the room in which they are being offered. The therapeutic alliance is therefore extraordinarily difficult to establish; any clinician attempting it must operate exclusively in the present-tense action register and let interpretation be inferred rather than spoken.
- **Tier 4 — People who have, in fact, lied to her.** The *Made in the USA* discovery that her foundational story was not what she had been told produces, briefly, the only behavior in her record that resembles betrayal-rage rather than betrayal-flight. Even there, the rage is short and is resolved by motion. She does not nurse grievance; she banks it and moves on.

Trust, when granted, is not graduated — it is binary and durable. Once admitted, a person retains the visa essentially forever unless they cross the bright-line moral perimeter (harm a vulnerable person, betray the cause). The visa does not, however, come with deeper access; admitted people get loyalty and presence, not interiority.

---

## 7.5 Betrayal: What She Counts as One, and What She Does With It

The subject's taxonomy of betrayal is idiosyncratic and important to map precisely, because it determines who she will and will not break with.

**Counted as betrayal:**
- Harming someone she has undertaken to protect.
- Lying to her about a *fact in the world* that bears on a mission or a moral choice.
- Pressuring her into stillness or into processing she has not consented to.
- Treating her like a child requiring management rather than a peer.

**NOT counted as betrayal, though they would be for most subjects:**
- Leaving her. (Leaving is the natural state of relationships in her schema; she has no standing to object to it.)
- Failing to know her. (She has not made herself known; she cannot resent the consequence.)
- Failing her in a crisis through ordinary human limitation. (She extends, to others, a generosity around fallibility she does not extend to herself.)

When she does experience betrayal, the response is not retaliatory; it is *terminal and quiet*. She does not deliver speeches; she removes the relationship from the active register. The betrayer is not punished — they are *no longer addressed*. This is the most ruthless register in her behavioral vocabulary and the one most likely to be misread by observers as indifference. It is not indifference. It is the same machinery that protected her from the Madres' abandonment turned outward: *if you can be lost, you can be pre-emptively absented*.

The exception, again, is the foundational lie about her origin. That betrayal she neither pre-emptively absents nor punishes; she absorbs it through dissociation and reconstruction. There is no one to break with — the betrayers are the dead, or the institution, or her own younger psyche. So the betrayal-machinery has no target and the system briefly stalls. This is the closest the subject comes to the kind of *unresolved* attachment behavior the AAI would code.

---

## 7.6 Repair: The Underdeveloped Capacity

Repair is the most poorly developed of the subject's relational capacities, and the reason is structural: repair requires sustained presence in the rupture, and her entire system is built to remove her from rupture. When she does repair — and she does, with Kate, with the Young Avengers across their cycles, eventually with Catalina — the repair has a characteristic shape:

- **Time, not talk.** She lets the calendar do the work. After a rupture she goes away (often dimensionally), allows weeks or months, and then reappears as though nothing decisive had occurred. The reappearance is the apology.
- **A small gift of presence.** The return is often marked by a small concrete gesture — showing up to help with a fight, dropping in for a meal, fixing something. The gesture is the content; she does not narrate it.
- **No naming of the rupture.** She will almost never say "I'm sorry I left." If pressed, she may produce a clipped acknowledgment, but she will not elaborate. The cost of elaboration is too high; the system reads it as the kind of processing it cannot tolerate.
- **Resumption of the prior register.** Once reception is granted, she resumes teasing-affection-shoulder-bump intimacy as if the relationship had been continuous.

This works with partners who accept it (Kate) and fails catastrophically with partners who do not (Lisa). With Lisa, the absence of explicit repair was experienced — correctly — as a refusal to be in the relationship. The subject is not capable, at her current developmental stage, of the kind of repair that named-and-processed adult intimacy requires. She is capable of *continuity through forgiveness she neither requests nor offers explicitly*. With the right counterparty this is enough. With most counterparties it is not.

---

## 7.7 Intimacy & Sexuality

Sexual identity is, as noted in §3, one of the genuinely unconflicted domains. The subject is canonically lesbian; she does not appear to have struggled with disclosure, internal acceptance, or community belonging in this dimension. Her flirting register is direct, declarative, slightly performative — the same swagger that operates in combat operates in seduction, with the same function (foreclosing the vulnerability of being seen wanting).

Sexual intimacy and emotional intimacy are, however, *decoupled* in her behavior in a way that is clinically significant. She can be sexually present and emotionally guarded simultaneously, and tends to be. With Lisa, the sexual relationship preceded and outlasted any successful emotional disclosure. The body is, again, the medium through which difficult states are processed and discharged — including the difficult state of being wanted. Sex is not avoided; *post-coital intimacy* (the conversation, the staying, the planning) is what triggers the avoidant protocols.

Dependency in the romantic frame is essentially absent. She does not lean on a partner for material support, emotional regulation, or planning. She does not ask a partner to choose her over their own commitments. She does not, conversely, accept being chosen — when Lisa restructured her life around the subject, the subject experienced it as encirclement rather than gift. This is the single most consistent obstacle to the subject's sustained romantic functioning and the most likely site of future rupture in any new partnership.

---

## 7.8 Friendship: The Kate Bishop Calibration

The friendship with Kate Bishop is the most successful sustained attachment in the record, and the reasons it works are precisely the reasons most others do not:

- Kate makes no demand for emotional disclosure. She accepts the subject's self-presentation as a working interface.
- Kate's own attachment style is sufficiently mobile that her presence does not constitute encirclement. They can not-see-each-other for long periods without rupture.
- The friendship is organized around shared *action* (cases, missions, fights) rather than shared *introspection*.
- Kate is permitted to tease, which the subject reads as affection, but not to interpret, which the subject would read as encroachment.
- Crucially, Kate has earned trust on both moral and competence axes, and the visa is permanent.

This dyad is the operational proof of what the subject is capable of when the relational structure matches her tolerance. It should be the template against which any future therapeutic alliance is designed.

---

## 7.9 Family of Origin / Family of Discovery

The relationships to the Madres (deceased, idealized), the grandmother Madrimar (revered, distanced), and the sister Catalina (the difficult living relative) form the family substrate. Each requires separate notation:

- **The Madres** function less as remembered persons than as an internalized moral standard. The subject does not appear to dream of them, intrude on them, or speak to them in private monologue; they exist as a *direction* (toward sacrifice, toward protection) rather than as figures. This is unusual and clinically informative — the loss has been so thoroughly converted into orientation that the persons have receded.
- **Madrimar** is held at exactly the distance the subject holds all elders: respect, deference on her terms, no requested guidance. The grandmother's wisdom is accepted when offered, not solicited.
- **Catalina** is the live wire. A sister is the one relationship that cannot be exited via portal without ongoing cost, because shared origin keeps reasserting the bond. The subject's behavior with Catalina shows more of the avoidance machinery under strain than any other dyad — she is forced to repeatedly approach what she has spent her life arranging not to approach. The relationship is, accordingly, the single most growth-productive in her current life, and the most uncomfortable.

---

## 7.10 Team Behavior: Loyalty Without Belonging

Across every team — Teen Brigade, Young Avengers, A-Force, Ultimates, West Coast Avengers — the subject's pattern is identical and worth stating cleanly: **she serves without joining.** She will fight harder for the team than members who consider themselves more permanently affiliated; she will also leave more easily. The loyalty is to the *mission* and to specific individuals on the team; it is not to the institution of the team itself.

She defaults to a leadership posture (as noted in §5) not from ambition but from low tolerance for indecision and from the operational habit of moving first. On teams with a designated leader, she is a difficult lieutenant — compliant on tactics, resistant on process, dismissive of any cohesion-building activity that requires sustained vulnerability. Team retreats, debriefs, and bonding rituals are, for her, the most aversive component of team membership. She would rather fight an unwinnable battle than attend a feelings circle.

---

## 7.11 The Template, Stated Once More for the Record

Every relationship in this subject's life is the same relationship, configured to a different counterparty: *I will arrive at speed, fight beside you, joke with you, defend you, and refuse to be known by you. I will leave before you leave, and I will return when leaving is no longer the question. I will not ask you for what I needed from the Madres, because to ask would be to admit that I needed it and did not get it. I will give you, instead, what they gave me — presence, protection, and eventual departure — and I will call this love, because in the only schema I have, it is.*

The subject is capable of more than this template permits. The evidence is in the moments she breaks it — the rare, brief disclosures with Kate, the difficult ongoing approach to Catalina, the dissociative-then-reconstructive response to her own destabilized history. The template is not destiny. It is, however, the operational baseline a surveillance file must assume, and the structure against which any change — therapeutic, relational, or self-generated — will have to be measured.


## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# DEFENSES & COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS

## Subject: America Chavez — Defensive Architecture, Full Inventory

---

The subject's defensive system is unusually *legible* for a trauma-organized personality, because it has been built almost entirely outward rather than inward. Where many CPTSD presentations construct their fortifications in interior space — repression, dissociation, somatic conversion held inside the skin — this subject externalizes nearly every defensive operation into the world. The defenses are kinetic, geographic, vocal, postural, and interpersonal. They can therefore be observed, mapped, and ranked with high confidence from the published record. What follows is the full inventory, ordered from most primitive (developmentally early, least mediated by reflection) to most mature (closest to genuine integrative function), with operational examples and the cost-benefit profile of each.

---

## I. PRIMITIVE DEFENSES (Pre-verbal / Pre-reflective)

### 1. Acting Out / Motoric Discharge

The most primitive and most frequently mobilized defense in the file. The structural rule: *any affect approaching conscious threshold is converted, within seconds, into gross motor activity.* The activity is most often locomotion (leaving the room, leaving the building, leaving the planet, leaving the timeline) or impact (a punch, a kick, a portal-kick through reality). The diagnostic *Young Avengers* sequence — punching Loki through successive realities — is not the comedy beat it reads as on the page; it is the subject discharging unbearable affect (the recognition of betrayal by a team member, in a peer group she had only ambivalently joined) into the only channel her nervous system has fully developed for processing.

The somatic-locomotive nature of her superpower makes this defense uniquely well-resourced. Most subjects with this pattern still face a friction cost — finding the door, getting to the car, booking the flight. The subject can convert affect to transit in under a second by kicking. The defense is therefore *frictionless* in a way that has prevented the development of more mature alternatives. There is no incentive to learn to sit with a feeling when the feeling can be outrun before it finishes arriving.

**Operational signature:** sudden shifts in posture (weight onto back foot, then onto the kicking leg), foreshortening of conversation mid-sentence, departure without verbal closure, return without verbal acknowledgment of departure. The pattern is so consistent across writers that it functions as a behavioral fingerprint.

### 2. Splitting

Operational and observable. The subject's moral universe is organized into clean categories — *those who protect* and *those who prey*, *those who arrive* and *those who abandon*, *those who can be trusted as-presented* and *those who require monitoring*. Once a person or institution is sorted into a category, re-sorting is rare and resisted. Loki is sorted into "predator/manipulator" on first contact and never substantially recategorized despite the team's gradual rapprochement. Authority figures sort to "suspect until earned." The Madres sort to "unimpeachable" with such force that any data threatening the sort produces decompensation rather than reconsideration.

The cost: complex others (those who are both supportive and demanding, both safe and frustrating, both like the Madres and unlike them) are flattened to one pole or quietly removed from the field of perception.

### 3. Denial — Specifically of Pain and Wear

The subject does not register injury at the level of self-narrative. The medical record (§2) documents combat damage in *America* #4–6 followed by immediate re-entry into action without convalescence. This is not stoicism in the classical sense; stoicism is endurance with acknowledgment. The subject's pattern is *non-registration* — the injury does not enter the inventory of self-states at all. "I do not get hurt" is held not as a boast but as a working operational premise. The denial extends to fatigue (no documented exhaustion sequences), emotional exhaustion (no documented withdrawal-for-recovery beyond strategic exits framed as agency), and, most consequentially, to the wear of unprocessed grief.

The cost is the one all such denials incur: the unregistered accumulates, and the system that has refused to inventory it will eventually be presented with the total bill in a context not of its choosing.

### 4. Somatization-in-Reverse (Affect → Action, never Affect → Body)

A specific variant worth distinguishing from generic acting-out. Classical somatization converts affect into bodily symptom (headache, gut, fatigue). This subject's pattern is the inverse: affect is converted into bodily *action*, but the body itself is held immune from symptomatic expression. There are no documented psychosomatic complaints. The body is the discharge instrument, never the symptom-bearer. This is a more primitive arrangement than somatization proper because it permits no signal — the body cannot even whisper that something is wrong; it can only swing.

---

## II. IMMATURE DEFENSES (Adolescent-Organized, Identity-Protective)

### 5. Counterphobic Confrontation

The defense that most reliably reads as a virtue. Where the trauma-template would predict avoidance of feared stimuli, the subject *moves toward* them — picks the fight, opens the door, kicks the portal into the threatening reality. The published examples are dense: punching Hitler, training with the warrior queens of the Utopian Parallel, taking on multiversal threats above her established tier. The function is to convert the fear-state, which is intolerable, into the action-state, which is familiar. The fear never gets to be a fear; it is intercepted at the threshold and reissued as a target.

This defense is highly adaptive in combat contexts and highly maladaptive in intimate ones, because intimacy presents fear-stimuli that *cannot be punched* — the disclosure that would deepen a relationship, the question that would reorganize a self-narrative, the silence that would let grief surface. Confronted with these, the counterphobic apparatus misfires: the subject "attacks" the situation by leaving it, by making a hard joke, by escalating the emotional tone past the point where the original tender stimulus can be re-approached.

### 6. Idealization (of the Madres, the Utopian Parallel, the Origin Myth)

The Madres are held in a sealed compartment marked unimpeachable. Their decision to die was *necessary*, their love *complete*, their sacrifice *meaningful*. The Utopian Parallel is held as a queer-utopian motherland, beautiful and outside time. The cost of this sealing is that the abandonment dimension of their choice — the fact that to a child, "the parents chose to die" is also "the parents chose to leave me" — cannot be examined without breaking the seal, and breaking the seal is felt (correctly, by the system's own internal logic) as catastrophic.

The *Made in the USA* arc is the diagnostic stress test: when the idealized origin is challenged by an alternate (medical-trauma) narrative, the subject does not negotiate between accounts. She experiences brief dissociation, then restabilizes by reasserting motion. Idealization here is not naïveté; it is *load-bearing*. Remove it without scaffolding and the structure shifts.

### 7. Devaluation (of those who fail her standards, of institutions, of process)

The dialectical partner of idealization. Persons or institutions that demand from her what she cannot give — sustained intimate processing, hierarchical deference, slow deliberative engagement — are quickly downgraded in her interior schema and treated with the dismissive register documented across team appearances. Lisa Halloran, who asked for the ordinary work of a relationship, was devalued not in moral terms but in *narrative weight* — written out of the subject's operating story rather than confronted. Academic authority at Sotomayor was similarly downgraded when it demanded stillness she could not produce. The devaluation is rarely cruel; it is functional, an efficiency mechanism that closes off demand vectors.

### 8. Grandiosity-in-Service-of-Competence

A specifically calibrated defense, distinct from narcissistic grandiosity. The subject's swagger is not a falsified self-assessment — she is, by the evidence, exactly as capable as she presents. The defensive use of the swagger lies not in inflating the self but in *foreclosing the conversations the self cannot tolerate*. The posture, vocal register, hand-on-hip stance, and declarative cadence collectively signal: *do not ask, do not soften, do not invite the vulnerable disclosure*. The grandiosity is a perimeter, not a fantasy. Its cost is that it makes the subject difficult to comfort even when comfort is what is wanted, and it teaches close others not to extend it.

### 9. Reaction Formation around Vulnerability

When tender material is in the air, the subject's first impulse is to produce its tonal opposite — a hard joke, a curt dismissal, a swagger-amplification, a physical gesture of unflappability. The reaction is fast enough to look like temperament; it is, on close reading, defense. Compare moments where Kate Bishop offers low-key emotional registration: the subject's reply is reliably one click harder than the register would invite. The function is to re-establish the perimeter that the offered tenderness was about to soften.

### 10. Identification with the Aggressor (Partial)

Present in attenuated form, specifically with respect to the Madres' template. The Madres "left" by an act of heroic sacrifice; the subject has organized her life around being the one who leaves by an act of heroic mobility. The structural mimicry is exact: I will not be the one who is left; I will be the one who departs for high purpose. The defense converts the unbearable position (abandoned child) into its inverse (sovereign departer). It is partial because the subject does not adopt the abandoner's affect or stance toward others wholesale; she adopts only the *leaving function*, and leaves with care, with returns, with affection intact at distance.

---

## III. NEUROTIC DEFENSES (Mid-level, Verbal-Symbolic)

### 11. Displacement (Geographic and Dimensional)

The subject does not redirect anger from boss to spouse to dog in the classical Freudian chain; she redirects internal states onto *locations*. Affect that should be processed in a relationship is processed by being elsewhere — a different country, a different planet, a different reality. The portal power makes displacement an essentially limitless resource.
