The "punching Hitler" sequence is a textbook instance: when the slow demands of college life produce affective overload, the subject displaces the overload onto a discrete, morally clean, historically dispatchable target in another timeline. She returns "regulated," but nothing in the original situation has been addressed.

### 12. Intellectualization — Limited and Selective

Present, but underdeveloped. The subject can articulate her own pattern in broad strokes ("I leave; that's what I do") but does not use the articulation to modify the pattern. Intellectualization here is a *naming* defense rather than an *analyzing* one — she can name the move once it has happened, which produces the appearance of insight while doing none of insight's work. This is the most-developed verbal-defensive register she has, and it is shallow by design.

### 13. Rationalization

Closely paired with the above. Exits from intimacy are rationalized as *missions* ("I'm needed elsewhere," "the multiverse won't wait," "I have to train"). The rationalizations are usually true at the factual level — there is always somewhere she is genuinely needed — which makes the defense unusually robust, because it never has to lie. The structure of multiversal heroism perfectly accommodates the avoidant pattern: there is always a legitimate reason to leave, and the reasons are morally unimpeachable.

### 14. Humor (Hard-Edged, Deflective)

Used regularly, almost always at the perimeter of a vulnerable disclosure. The humor is sardonic, declarative, often self-aggrandizing in a wink-bearing register that simultaneously establishes competence and forecloses sincerity. It is not the integrative humor of the mature defenses (which would acknowledge the vulnerability while making it bearable); it is *deflective* humor, which uses the laugh to change the channel.

---

## IV. MATURE DEFENSES (Integrative, Genuinely Adaptive)

### 15. Sublimation into Protective Action

The most genuinely mature defense in her inventory, and the one that does the most actual work. The unmetabolized grief and rage of the original abandonment are channeled into a sustained, principled, multi-decade pattern of *interposing herself between predators and the vulnerable*. The sublimation is not perfect — it does not heal what it draws on — but it converts the unbearable into the world-improving with high reliability and at relatively low collateral cost. Marginalized people across multiple realities have, demonstrably, been protected because the subject converted private wound into public service. This is the defense that justifies the rest; it is also the one that makes the rest seem unnecessary, which is its own trap.

### 16. Altruism (Genuine, Pre-reflective)

Distinct from sublimation in that it is reflexive and undefended — she does not appear to weigh whether to help. The altruism is *constitutional* by this point in her development; whether it began as a defense or as a temperamental given, it now operates as a stable virtue. It is one of the unconflicted domains.

### 17. Loyalty (Specifically, Loyalty-at-Distance)

A bespoke mature defense, calibrated to her exact constraints. The subject has solved the problem of "I want community but cannot tolerate captivity" by developing a high-fidelity loyalty that operates *across distance and absence*. Kate Bishop is the canonical example: the friendship is real, deep, and durable, and it survives long separations and asynchronous communication precisely because Kate accepts the loyalty in the form the subject can sustain. This is genuinely adaptive — it produces real attachment without triggering the deactivating defenses — and it represents the subject's most sophisticated negotiation between her attachment need and her attachment fear.

### 18. Suppression (Tactical, Not Repressive)

Occasionally observed: the subject deliberately sets aside an affect *temporarily* to complete an operational task, with intent to return to it. The intent-to-return is usually not honored, which converts suppression into something closer to denial; but the suppression in the moment is mature in form, demonstrating that the capacity exists. With scaffolding, this is the defense most likely to be developable into a route toward integration.

---

## V. ADAPTIVE COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS (Positive)

Beyond the formal defenses, the subject has developed a series of compensatory mechanisms that function as *life-resources* rather than perimeter-walls. These deserve separate inventory because they are her strengths, and because any therapeutic or relational engagement with the subject must work with them rather than past them.

- **Code-switching into Spanish for emotional emphasis.** A genuine compensatory mechanism. Spanish carries the affective load that English-language swagger forecloses. When the subject switches registers, she is permitting a fraction of the affect to surface inside a linguistic container that feels safer (associated, plausibly, with the Madres and the Utopian/Washington Heights mother-tongue substrate). This is one of the few channels in which interior states reach exterior expression without immediately being converted to motion.
- **Embodied joy.** The swagger is partly defense and partly *real pleasure in her own competence and form*. The subject genuinely enjoys her body, her power, her capacity to move through space and reality. This joy is not feigned and not derivative; it is a stable positive affect that the trauma has not colonized.
- **Moral clarity.** The bright-line ethical compass operates as a compensatory cognitive structure that simplifies the decision-load and frees attention for action. It is not philosophically sophisticated, but it is operationally robust and rarely produces the wrong call on first-order questions of harm.
- **Selective receptivity.** The subject can receive care from a narrow band of people (Kate, occasionally Madrimar, occasionally a teammate who has met her on her terms long enough to be trusted). This is small, but it is real, and it is the seed of any future expansion.
- **Pride in identity (queer, Latina, powered).** Stable, integrated, and unconflicted — a genuine identity resource that the trauma has not destabilized. The unconflictedness of these domains provides the platform from which the conflicted domains might, eventually, be approached.
- **Capacity for principled refusal.** She can say no to power, to coercion, to bad orders, and to bad faith. This is a mature capacity, not a reactive one, and it is one of the cleanest things about her.

---

## VI. MALADAPTIVE COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS (Negative)

- **Serial exits from intimacy.** The pattern dressed as agency. Each exit is locally defensible; the aggregate cost is a relational landscape thinner than it should be by this point in her life.
- **Premature certainty.** The verdict-style cognition closes inquiry before it can yield surprise. Useful in combat, costly in self-knowledge.
- **Weaponization of confidence.** The swagger used to foreclose, not just to assert. Close others learn not to ask.
- **Memory-editing at the structural level.** The most consequential maladaptive compensatory mechanism in the file. The *Made in the USA* record suggests that under sufficient early pressure, the subject's defensive apparatus is capable of overwriting autobiographical memory itself — replacing unbearable material with a coherent alternative narrative. This is not lying; it is a system-level operation that runs below introspective access. The cost is that the subject does not fully know her own history, and the defenses are protecting a story she did not author and cannot fully verify.
- **Avoidance of stillness.** Stillness would be the entry point to integration. The system has been built to make stillness aversive. The subject is therefore structurally prevented from accessing the very condition in which growth would occur.
- **Compulsive mobility.** The portal power as addiction-substrate. Every difficulty has a frictionless exit, and the frictionlessness teaches the system to use the exit before the difficulty has been registered as such.

---

## VII. SYNTHESIS — THE DEFENSIVE ARCHITECTURE AS A SINGLE STRUCTURE

Read together, the defenses describe a coherent, beautifully engineered system whose central operating principle is *the conversion of interior states into exterior motion before the interior state can be felt as such*. Primitive layers (acting out, denial, splitting) intercept affect at the threshold. Immature layers (counterphobic confrontation, idealization-devaluation, grandiosity) protect the self-narrative that the primitive layers have produced. Neurotic layers (displacement, rationalization, deflective humor) provide the verbal-symbolic scaffolding that makes the whole structure socially legible and morally defensible. Mature layers (sublimation, altruism, loyalty-at-distance) convert the defensive output into genuine prosocial work, which validates the system from outside and renders it durable.

The system's brilliance is its self-justification: every defense produces, as byproduct, something the world wants more of — protection, courage, principled action, durable friendship at distance. The system's tragedy is that it has no native pathway to the interior, and the one event that could open such a pathway (sustained stillness in the presence of a safe other) is precisely the event the system is most efficiently organized to prevent.

She is, on the evidence, exactly as defended as she needs to be to keep functioning, and exactly as defended as prevents her from finishing the work the original wound demands. The architecture is not failing; it is succeeding at what it was built to do. The question for any future engagement is not how to dismantle it — it is load-bearing and the subject is not currently in a position to survive its dismantling — but how to introduce, slowly, a single new defense capable of holding interior material without converting it to motion. Suppression-with-honored-return is the candidate. Everything else follows from whether that capacity can be grown.


## Longitudinal Psychological Profile

# LONGITUDINAL PSYCHOLOGICAL PROFILE

## America Chavez — Decade-by-Decade Clinical Picture

A note on method before the file: the subject's published record is compressed (≈2011–present) but the *in-universe* developmental span it depicts is wider — early childhood in the contested origin site (Washington Heights and/or the Utopian Parallel), pre-adolescent power-onset, an adolescent vigilante phase (*Vengeance*, Teen Brigade), young-adult team membership (*Young Avengers*, Ultimates, A-Force, West Coast Avengers), the college-era attempted normalization (*America* solo), and the recent recontextualization of the entire narrative substrate (*Made in the USA*). What follows reads each developmental window as its own clinical snapshot — affect, cognition, self-concept — and tracks the slope of change between them. The headline finding, stated up front: the affect-regulation system has been remarkably stable across the entire arc; the cognitive style has narrowed in some respects and matured in others; and the self-concept is the only domain that has undergone genuine, painful, incomplete revision.

---

## I. Childhood Window (Pre-Powers Through Power-Onset; In-Universe Reconstruction Only)

No first-person record exists from this window — every depiction is reconstructive, filtered through the subject's later narrative (the Utopian Parallel story) or through the *Made in the USA* retcon (Washington Heights, the Santana procedure, Catalina). The clinical interest is precisely in *which* version the adult subject preferentially reports, and what that preference indicates.

**Affect regulation (inferred).** The pediatric-medical-trauma framing from *Made in the USA* — repeated procedures, the Edge League program, a sibling who was either lost, separated, or unacknowledged — is consistent with the early establishment of *dissociative segregation* as a primary regulatory tool: the unbearable affect is not modulated, it is partitioned away from the experiencing self entirely. The Utopian Parallel myth then functions as the *positive content* layered over the partition. This is a Type II / chronic-trauma profile (Terr) rather than a single-incident response, and it would explain the adult subject's near-total absence of classical intrusion symptoms — the original material was sequestered structurally, not merely repressed.

**Cognitive style (inferred).** The adult subject's bright-line moral cognition and verdict-first reasoning are most parsimoniously read as a child's defensive simplification of an environment in which adults were either dangerous (clinicians, the program) or absent (the lost/dying mother-figures, in whichever version). A child who must rapidly classify caregivers as safe / unsafe with no margin for nuance develops exactly the dichotomous schema the adult subject still operates from.

**Self-concept (inferred).** The foundation laid in this window is the one she has been defending ever since: *I am the kind of person to whom the worst thing already happened, and I survived it gloriously.* The grandiose-survivor identity is laid in early enough that it pre-dates the introspective capacity that would later be required to revise it.

---

## II. Adolescent / Early-Vigilante Window (*Vengeance*, Teen Brigade, ≈Ages 14–17)

This is the first window with direct behavioral evidence. The Casey-era subject is already, in essential structure, the adult subject — which is itself a clinical datum. There is no observable adolescent identity diffusion, no experimental phase, no try-on of alternative selves. The "Miss America" presentation arrives fully formed.

**Affect regulation.** Almost entirely *externalized and kinetic*. The Teen Brigade arc shows a subject who manages internal arousal by entering and exiting situations at speed, who uses combat as a baseline state rather than an escalation, and who gum-snaps, posture-shifts, and code-switches as low-level discharge channels between fights. In a developmental window where peers would be experimenting with talk-based regulation (best-friend confessional, journaling, the affective vocabulary of pop music), the subject is already on a purely behavioral track. Linehan's framework is useful: distress tolerance is *enormous*; emotion regulation in the technical sense (labeling, modulating, communicating affect) is *severely underdeveloped*. The asymmetry — the adolescent who can take a Thor-tier hit but cannot name a feeling — is the signature.

**Cognitive style.** Concrete-operational with sharp threat-pattern recognition and poor mentalization of non-threatening others. She reads Teen Brigade peers as either useful or in-the-way; she does not appear to wonder what they want, fear, or hope. This is *not* a deficit of intelligence — it is a deficit of attentional allocation. Mentalizing requires sustained attention to ambiguous interior states; her attentional system is tuned for fast classification of exterior threat.

**Self-concept.** Maximally consolidated for the developmental window. Most adolescents in identity-status terms (Marcia) are in moratorium or diffusion; the subject is in a precocious *foreclosed* status — identity adopted without crisis, defended without exploration. The Utopian Parallel narrative is the foreclosed content. The clinical risk of foreclosure is that the eventual crisis, when it comes, is more destabilizing than a crisis met during normative moratorium would have been. This is foreshadowed and eventually realized in *Made in the USA*.

---

## III. Young-Adult Team Window (*Young Avengers*, Gillen, ≈Ages 17–19)

The Gillen run is the densest behavioral record of how the subject functions in a *peer system that demands processing*. The team's structure — Loki manipulating affect, Wiccan and Hulkling's relational center of gravity, Kate Bishop's wry mediation, Prodigy's anxious empathy — is exactly the kind of intimate, talk-heavy environment her regulatory system is unequipped for. Her response is the clinical centerpiece of the decade.

**Affect regulation.** Continues to be kinetic-externalized, now with *interpersonal exit* added as a major channel. She arrives mid-crisis, refuses cohesion rituals, leaves and returns on her own schedule. Mikulincer & Shaver's *deactivation strategies* literature on dismissive-avoidant attachment maps onto this almost perfectly: suppression of attachment-system activation via distancing, devaluation of the necessity of others, and compulsive self-reliance. The Loki sequences are diagnostically rich — she is the *only* member who clocks him early because her threat-detection apparatus is hypertrophied and uncorrupted by attachment hunger. The team's affectively-attached members are blinded; she is not. The price of the clarity is that she cannot use the team for what the team is for.

**Cognitive style.** Still verdict-first, still threat-tuned, but now operating in a peer environment that occasionally rewards her for it (the Loki call) and occasionally penalizes her for it (her dismissal of Prodigy, her brusqueness with Wiccan). There is the first evidence of *meta-cognitive learning*: by the end of the run she demonstrates incremental tolerance for the team's emotional pace, even if she does not adopt it. This is the first observable plasticity in the file.

**Self-concept.** The Utopian narrative is fully operational and used as social capital — she introduces herself by it, deploys it to establish hierarchy, and uses it to foreclose questions about her past. The team accepts the narrative at face value, which both stabilizes her and forecloses the developmental work she might otherwise have done. The window ends with the self-concept intact and the relational repertoire only marginally expanded.

---

## IV. Inter-Team Drift Window (Ultimates, A-Force, *West Coast Avengers* Appearances, ≈Ages 19–20)

A shorter window characterized by *serial team membership without consolidation*. Clinically, this is the avoidant pattern at its most operationally visible. The subject is in motion: she joins teams that suit her current mood and exits when retention pressure accumulates.

**Affect regulation.** Unchanged in mechanism, more sophisticated in deployment. She has learned which environments tolerate her exits (Ultimates' high-concept cosmic frame demands little intimacy; A-Force's mission-focus respects her competence) and which do not (the slower-tempo team-bonding contexts she is shown declining). This is selection-as-regulation — choosing environments compatible with the regulatory system she has, rather than developing new regulatory skills.

**Cognitive style.** Some maturation: she demonstrates strategic patience in the Ultimates' cosmic-scale problems she cannot punch — there is observable tolerance for working through a non-kinetic plan, at least in short bursts. The threat-tuning extends to ontological threats (entropy, multiversal collapse) rather than just personal-scale ones. This is a real cognitive broadening.

**Self-concept.** Still the Utopian survivor-hero. Reinforced rather than challenged by these team environments, all of which credential her on her own terms.

---

## V. College / Attempted Normalization Window (*America* Solo, Rivera, ≈Age 20)

This is the window in which the subject *deliberately tries to live a normative young-adult life* — and the file's richest demonstration that the regulatory system she has built is incompatible with that life. Sotomayor University is the experimental condition; her decompensation profile under it is the dependent variable.

**Affect regulation.** Under sustained low-grade demand for stillness (lectures, sustained dyadic intimacy with Lisa, ordinary college-administrative pacing), the regulatory system *runs out of channels*. She cannot kinetically discharge in a lecture hall without consequence. The result is the predictable cascade: irritability, increased code-switching into Spanish (a partial regulatory channel — emotive language allows some discharge even when the body cannot move), micro-exits (leaving lectures), and eventually macro-exits (interdimensional sorties framed as missions, e.g., the "punch Hitler" excursions). The framing of those sorties as heroic moral action is genuine *and* is the rationalization layer over what is structurally a flight response. From a DBT lens: distress tolerance remains high, emotion regulation is observably failing under chronic-low-grade-demand conditions in a way it does not fail under acute-high-demand combat conditions.

**Cognitive style.** Most regression observed in the entire file. The verdict-first style, which had been broadening in the team windows, narrows back down. Classroom material requires *sustained ambiguity-tolerance* — exactly the cognitive mode she has least developed. She does not lack the intellect; she lacks the cognitive-attentional patience the environment requires. She solves it by absenting herself rather than by recruiting the patience.

**Relational evidence.** The Lisa Halloran relationship is the most clinically informative dyad in the file. Lisa is not threatening, not demanding, not pathological — she is *available*, which is the most threatening configuration the subject's attachment system encounters. The subject cannot tolerate the steady-state proximity; the relationship dissolves through her serial absences. Fonagy's mentalization-based framework is apt: the subject's capacity to hold Lisa's interior state in mind while also experiencing her own is impaired; she defaults to pre-mentalized modes (teleological — "if I leave and come back with a trophy, that is love"; psychic-equivalence — "if I feel cornered, I am cornered"). The relationship's failure is not Lisa's and not, in any moral sense, the subject's — it is the predictable output of an attachment system that has never been remediated.

**Self-concept.** First serious destabilization. The Madrimar arc reveals the Utopian Parallel was, in part, a constructed narrative. The subject's response is the *Made in the USA* response in miniature: brief dissociation, then re-stabilization through action. She does not metabolize the destabilization; she absorbs it as one more datum about which she will not think.

---

## VI. Confabulation-Collapse Window (*Made in the USA*, Vazquez, Present)

The window in which the foundational narrative is contested at full strength. The Washington Heights material surfaces; the medical-experimentation history is named; Catalina exists. The subject is forced into proximity with the architecture of her own defenses.

**Affect regulation.** Under the most acute self-concept pressure of her life, the regulatory system shows its first true *Stage 4* signature — brief dissociative episodes, the kind that had been structurally sequestered since childhood. This is clinically significant: the partition (§I) is permeable under sufficient pressure. The system she built was never designed to process the original material; it was designed to *prevent* its return. The fact that the return is occurring at all means the partition is failing — and the failure is, paradoxically, the precondition for any genuine integration.

**Cognitive style.** The most painful broadening yet. She is being asked to hold *two histories simultaneously* — the Utopian narrative she has organized her life around and the Washington Heights narrative that may be truer. Holding two incompatible narratives without immediate resolution is exactly the ambiguity-tolerance her cognitive style was built to refuse. She is doing it badly, partially, with frequent collapses into action — but she is doing it.

**Self-concept.** The first *real* identity work of her life. In Marcia's terms, this is the belated moratorium that the foreclosed adolescent identity skipped — only now arriving in young adulthood, under maximum pressure, with the additional load of an entire constructed self to dismantle. The instability is appropriate to the task. The subject's residual stable domains — sexuality, ethnic and linguistic identity, physical competence, the moral spine — are doing the load-bearing work that allows the conflicted domain (history, origin, the Madres) to undergo revision without total collapse. This is the structural reason she is surviving the window: the unconflicted scaffolding is strong enough to hold while the conflicted core is rebuilt.

---

## VII. Cross-Window Synthesis: What Has Changed, What Has Not

**Affect regulation.** Mechanism unchanged across the entire arc — externalized, kinetic, exit-as-regulation. Sophistication of deployment increased markedly (better environment-selection, better discrimination between situations that tolerate her style and those that do not). Failure mode unchanged: chronic-low-grade-stillness demand defeats the system. Emerging signal: the Stage 4 dissociative episodes in the present window are the first evidence the system is being stressed past its design tolerance — clinically a *good* sign for the possibility of remediation, a *bad* sign for short-term stability.

**Cognitive style.** Real broadening over time in the *operational* domain (cosmic-scale strategy, multi-step planning under threat) and real broadening, recently and painfully, in the *autobiographical* domain (holding two histories at once). No meaningful broadening in the *interpersonal-mentalization* domain — she still reads ambiguous others poorly, still defaults to verdict over inquiry. This is the most plausible site for targeted growth and the least likely site for spontaneous development.

**Self-concept.** The only domain that has undergone genuine, structural change — and only recently, only under maximum pressure, only partially. The trajectory from precocious-foreclosed (adolescent window) through socially-reinforced-stable (team windows) through first-destabilization (college window) through active-revision (present window) is a coherent developmental arc, just badly out of phase with chronological age. She is doing in her early twenties the identity work most subjects do in mid-adolescence, with the additional difficulty that her foreclosed identity was load-bearing in a way most adolescent identities are not.

**The structural constant.** Through every window, in every team configuration, under every name, the subject's organizing principle has been the same: *be the one who arrives, never the one left behind; be the one who leaves, never the one who needs.* Every cognitive style, every regulatory channel, every self-concept revision has been a variation on that single sustained answer to the foundational abandonment. The clinical question for the next window of the file is whether the present destabilization will permit the principle itself to be revised — whether the subject can eventually tolerate being, on some occasions, *the one who stays*. Nothing in the prior record predicts she can. Nothing in the present record proves she cannot. The file remains open.


## Psychiatric Assessment & Differential

# PSYCHIATRIC ASSESSMENT & DIFFERENTIAL

## Subject: America Chavez / "Miss America"
### Section 4 — Full Diagnostic Workup

---

## 4.1 Framing the Assessment

A psychiatric assessment of this subject must be conducted with an explicit caveat that ordinary diagnostic instruments were calibrated for a population that does not include children raised in (or told they were raised in) a pocket reality outside time, does not include subjects whose primary affective discharge route is kicking holes in the membrane of the multiverse, and does not include subjects whose foundational autobiographical memory has been demonstrably edited at the level of *content*, not merely affect. The DSM-5-TR and ICD-11 frameworks are nevertheless usable, because the subject's symptom architecture is recognizably human even where her circumstances are not. Powers do not exempt one from nosology; they only change the morphology of the symptom expression. A subject who manages dysregulation by leaving the timeline is using the same neural circuit as a subject who walks out of an argument — only the radius of the avoidance differs.

The assessment that follows draws on the full published record (Casey 2011 onward, *Young Avengers* 2013, *America* 2017, *Made in the USA* 2021, team appearances in *West Coast Avengers*, *Ultimates*, *Avengers Forever*, and tertiary crossover material). Where the *Made in the USA* retcon and the Utopian Parallel origin contradict, both are treated as psychologically operative: the subject *believed* one for most of her published life and *learned of* the other in adulthood, and the discordance between the two is itself diagnostic data.

---

## 4.2 Primary Diagnosis

### **Complex Post-Traumatic Stress Disorder** (ICD-11 6B41)
*With prominent avoidance-via-action presentation, attenuated intrusion symptoms, and partial dissociative amnesia for the index trauma.*

This is the single best-fit formulation, and it accounts for more of the longitudinal behavioral data than any combination of alternative diagnoses. The three ICD-11 CPTSD pillars beyond the core PTSD criteria are all present:

**(1) Disturbances in self-organization / negative self-concept.** The surface presentation is the opposite of negative self-concept — it is grandiose, declarative, "I am the one who arrives." But CPTSD self-concept disturbance is not synonymous with low self-esteem; it is *instability and incoherence of self-narrative*. The subject meets this criterion in the strongest possible form: her foundational autobiography was, per *Made in the USA*, partly a confabulation. Whether one accepts that retcon literally or reads it as metaphor for the way trauma victims construct mythic personal histories, the diagnostic implication is the same — the self-narrative is *load-bearing but not load-tested*, and when tested it produces the brief dissociative episodes observed in the Vazquez arc rather than ordinary doubt or curiosity.

**(2) Disturbances in relationships.** Catalogued in §3. Serial entries-and-exits from teams (Young Avengers joined and quit repeatedly, Ultimates joined and quit, West Coast joined and quit); the Lisa Halloran relationship dissolving under the weight of avoidant pattern; the singular sustained attachment to Kate Bishop being structurally enabled by Kate's low-demand profile. The pattern is not "cannot form bonds" — she forms them readily — it is "cannot tolerate the bond's gravity," which is the precise CPTSD signature, not a personality-disordered one.

**(3) Affect dysregulation.** Present, but expressed *kinetically and externally* rather than via the more commonly catalogued internalizing signs. Where a more typical CPTSD presentation might produce somatic complaints, dissociative numbing, or self-harm, this subject's regulation routes through gross motor discharge — flight, portal-creation, locomotion. This is not absence of dysregulation; it is dysregulation that has been *successfully shunted* into a physical channel by a body unusually well-equipped to handle it. The "successfully" is medically relative: the shunt prevents acute crises and produces a high-functioning operator, but it leaves the underlying affect unmetabolized and the introspective vocabulary undeveloped.

### Etiology

The etiological stack, in causal order:

1. **Pre-verbal / early-childhood loss of both primary caregivers** under circumstances framed to the child as heroic sacrifice. This is the irreducible kernel. Whether the Madres existed in the Utopian Parallel as originally narrated or were rewritten figures in the *Made in the USA* schema, the developmental fact is constant: the subject lost both attachment figures young, and the loss was packaged as their *choice*. A child cannot metabolize "they chose to leave me" without supportive interpretation; absent that, the child constructs interpretation independently — typically by identifying with the lost objects ("I will be the kind of person they were") and disavowing the abandonment ("they did not leave me; they *saved* me").

2. **Plausible pediatric medical trauma** per the *Made in the USA* substrate — experimental procedures producing the powers. Pediatric medical trauma is one of the most reliably documented producers of CPTSD-spectrum presentation in the clinical literature, and it produces precisely the symptom cluster observed: high pain tolerance (somatized), distrust of institutional authority, kinetic restlessness, and — crucially — *narrative reconstruction of the trauma into a more bearable form*, which is what the Utopian confabulation literally is on the Vazquez reading.

3. **Migratory / dimensional instability across formative years.** Even on the more benign Utopian reading, the subject left her origin reality young, traversed multiple environments, and lacked a stable adult-scaffolded developmental container. Disrupted environment compounds the attachment injury.

4. **Absent or intermittent corrective adult presence.** No sustained mentor figure across the published record. The grandmother (Madrimar) appears late and the relationship is conflicted. The subject essentially raised herself into her capabilities, which produces precocious competence and predictable gaps in self-regulation skill.

### Symptom Presentation in Behavior

Mapped to the standard PTSD/CPTSD symptom domains:

- **Re-experiencing:** Markedly attenuated. No documented nightmares, no flashback sequences in the classical sense, no panic-attack morphology. The closest analog is the dissociative episode in *Made in the USA* when the Utopian narrative is destabilized — a brief depersonalization-flavored stutter, not a sensory intrusion. The absence of classical intrusion is itself diagnostic: it is evidence that the avoidance defenses are operating *upstream* of intrusion, at the memory-access level rather than the memory-suppression level. This is the same mechanism that, in extremis, produces dissociative amnesia.

- **Avoidance:** Florid and pervasive. Behavioral avoidance of stillness, of intimate processing conversations, of any environment that requires sustained interior attention (Sotomayor lectures, romantic relationship maintenance, team check-ins). Cognitive avoidance via narrative reconstruction. Spatial avoidance via the portal capability, which converts ordinary "leave the room" into "leave the cosmos." The avoidance is so total and so successful that it has shaped the personality.

- **Hyperarousal:** Present but constrained. Threat-detection is sharp (Loki detection in *Young Avengers* is the cleanest example); baseline irritability under stress is documented; sleep disturbance not depicted, which may reflect underreporting rather than absence. Startle response not formally observable in the medium.

- **Negative alterations in cognition and mood:** Subtle. The subject does not present as anhedonic, and small-pleasure capacity is intact (the swagger contains genuine joy). What is altered is the *introspective channel itself* — affect labeling is impoverished, emotional vocabulary is action-vocabulary, and the subject does not appear to have an internal monologue oriented toward feeling-states.

- **Disturbances in self-organization (the C in CPTSD):** Discussed above. The grandiosity-over-fragility structure is the hallmark.

### Course Over Time

Across roughly a decade of published continuity, the course is *stable-chronic without remission and without progression to crisis*. The subject does not deteriorate; she also does not heal. This is a classic CPTSD trajectory in subjects who have constructed a high-functioning compensatory architecture early and have not been pressed into circumstances that exceed it. The *Made in the USA* arc represents the closest the subject has come to a clinically significant destabilization, and her response — brief dissociation, rapid re-stabilization through action, no sustained processing — is precisely what one would predict from the formulation. There is no documented therapeutic intervention; spontaneous remission of CPTSD without intervention is rare, and the subject's longitudinal stability of symptoms is consistent with rarity.

A note on prognosis: the system is robust against acute decompensation but brittle against *prolonged stillness or coerced introspection*. A scenario in which the subject is held immobile, deprived of kinetic discharge, and pressed on the foundational narrative would be the predicted decompensation vector — and the predicted decompensation morphology would be *dissociative*, not depressive or psychotic.

---

## 4.3 Comorbidity

### **Provisional / Subclinical: Avoidant features within an attachment-disordered presentation.**
Not a diagnosable Avoidant Personality Disorder — she does not avoid contact out of fear of judgment, which is the AVPD signature; she avoids *captivity by contact*, which is the dismissive-avoidant attachment signature. The distinction matters: AVPD subjects want closeness and fear it; this subject permits closeness and exits when its gravity exceeds tolerance. Code as *attachment pattern* (dismissive-avoidant), not as PD.

### **Provisional: Subclinical traits in the narcissistic-counterphobic neighborhood.**
Grandiosity present; sense of specialness present (she does come from a different reality and does have unique capabilities, which complicates the assessment — grandiosity is not pathological when it is approximately accurate); devaluation of those who fail her standards present. *But:* empathy is intact and operative, particularly toward the marginalized; the grandiosity is in service of competence and protection rather than supply-seeking; admiration is not sought and is often refused. This does not meet NPD threshold. The traits are *trauma-adaptive*, recruited into service of the avoidance architecture, and are predicted to attenuate if the underlying CPTSD were addressed.

### **Rule-in for differential consideration: Disorganized attachment with dismissive-avoidant overlay.**
Not a DSM diagnosis but a clinically meaningful descriptor. The subject's attachment history (loss of both primary figures under sacrifice-framed circumstances) is the precise developmental insult that produces disorganized attachment; her adult presentation is the dismissive-avoidant phenotype that disorganized children often grow into when the environment rewards self-reliance and competence.

### **Not present:** Substance use disorder, mood disorder of any episodic morphology, anxiety disorder of independent clinical significance, eating disorder, OCD-spectrum, psychotic-spectrum, neurodevelopmental disorder.

---

## 4.4 Rigorous Differential — What She Is Not, And Why

### **Not Posttraumatic Stress Disorder (simple PTSD, DSM-5).**
She has a trauma history and trauma sequelae, but the symptom profile fits the *complex* form rather than the simple form. Simple PTSD is organized around a discrete, often adult-onset traumatic event with prominent intrusion and hyperarousal; her presentation is organized around chronic developmental insult with prominent self- and relational-organization disturbance and attenuated intrusion. The CPTSD frame captures her more accurately and predicts her course better.

### **Not Major Depressive Disorder, recurrent or chronic.**
No documented anhedonia, no documented sustained low mood, no documented neurovegetative cluster. Baseline affect is dysphoric-irritable *under stress* but reverts cleanly when kinetic discharge is available. Hedonic capacity is intact — the gum-snapping, the visible enjoyment of competence, the social warmth toward Kate Bishop and toward the people she protects, all indicate a functioning reward system. The subject is wounded but not depressed. Confusing the two is a common clinical error in trauma assessment.

### **Not Bipolar I, II, or Cyclothymic Disorder.**
The high-energy, declarative, kinetic presentation could be misread as hypomanic if the longitudinal record were sampled briefly. It is not. There is no episodicity. The baseline *is* high-energy; there are no documented depressive crashes; sleep is not reduced in service of goal-directed activity; pressured speech is not observed (her speech is declarative and clipped, not pressured); grandiosity is not episodically inflated but constitutively present and approximately reality-calibrated. The cardinal feature of bipolar disorders — *change from baseline* — is absent. This is her baseline.

### **Not Attention-Deficit/Hyperactivity Disorder.**
The candidate symptoms — lecture-hall restlessness, low tolerance for sustained passive attention, action-bias, impulsivity — are real and would, in a clinic that did not take a trauma history, plausibly support an ADHD label. They should not. The restlessness is context-dependent in a way ADHD restlessness is not: she can sustain *threat-relevant* attention for arbitrarily long periods (combat, tactical assessment, protective vigilance), and her attentional collapse is specific to environments that require her to be still with her own interior. ADHD-driven restlessness does not discriminate between contexts in this way. The parsimonious explanation is that stillness permits affect emergence, affect emergence is intolerable, and the body therefore refuses stillness. This is trauma physiology, not attentional architecture.

### **Not Antisocial Personality Disorder, and not subclinical antisocial traits of clinical concern.**
Aggression is present and instrumental, but it is *morally organized* — directed at oppressors, calibrated to threat, never predatory, never deceptive, never for personal gain. Conscience is florid and operative. Remorse capacity is present where she has caused harm. The deception necessary for ASPD is absent; she is, if anything, pathologically direct. Categorical rule-out.

### **Not Narcissistic Personality Disorder.**
Discussed under comorbidity. Trait-level features present, syndrome-level diagnosis not supported. The decisive evidence is the operative empathy toward the marginalized — NPD-level grandiosity is not compatible with the depth and consistency of her protective orientation toward people who cannot reciprocate with admiration or status.

### **Not Borderline Personality Disorder.**
The avoidant pattern superficially could be mistaken for BPD's push-pull, but the morphology is wrong. BPD push-pull is driven by abandonment terror producing alternating clinging and rage; this subject's pattern is *unilaterally* avoidant, with no clinging phase and no abandonment-rage phase. She does not have identity diffusion in the BPD sense (her identity is *stable but partially confabulated*, which is a different structure). She does not have affective lability of the BPD type (rapid mood shifts within hours). She does not self-harm. She does not exhibit the BPD interpersonal hypersensitivity profile. Rule out.

### **Not Dissociative Identity Disorder, and not Other Specified Dissociative Disorder of identity-fragmentation type.**
Identity is unitary across the published record. The brief depersonalization episodes in *Made in the USA* are stress-precipitated and self-limiting; they do not indicate alternate identity structures. The fact that her *autobiographical narrative* was partially confabulated is not the same as identity fragmentation — confabulated history is consistent with a single integrated identity holding a partially false past, which is what trauma-driven narrative reconstruction typically produces.

### **Not Autism Spectrum Disorder.**
The candidate symptoms — low patience for ritual social processing, directness bordering on bluntness, preference for action over discussion — could be misread. They should not be. Social-cognitive capacity is intact (she reads people accurately when she chooses to attend to them); reciprocal social pleasure is intact (Kate Bishop friendship); sensory profile is unremarkable; restricted-interest pattern is absent; the developmental history necessary for ASD diagnosis is incompatible with the documented trajectory. The bluntness is trauma-adaptive impatience with processing, not neurodevelopmental difference in social cognition.

### **Not Schizophrenia-spectrum or any psychotic disorder.**
No positive symptoms, no negative symptoms, no formal thought disorder. The multiverse is, in her operational universe, literally real and literally walkable; her statements about traveling to other realities are accurate, not delusional. The single clinical caution here is that a clinician unfamiliar with her operational context could misclassify accurate accounts of dimensional travel as psychotic content. This is a documentation issue, not a diagnostic one.

### **Not Adjustment Disorder.**
The symptom complex is chronic and pre-dates any identifiable proximal stressor; not adjustment.

### **Not a primary substance-use disorder.**
Social drinking in college-era stories with no pattern suggestive of use disorder. Rule out.

---

## 4.5 Risk Profile, Restated With Diagnostic Specificity

- **Self-harm:** Low. No ideation documented; no behavioral indicators; trauma response is externalizing-kinetic, not internalizing.
- **Predatory or instrumental violence:** Near zero. Aggression is reactive, morally organized, and conscience-bound.
- **Reactive violence under threat to others:** High, and *appropriately calibrated*. This is not a risk; it is a feature of the protective architecture.
- **Flight under sustained relational pressure:** High. Predicted morphology — depart the room, the city, the planet, or the timeline, depending on intensity. This is the modal stress response.
- **Decompensation under coerced stillness or coerced narrative-challenge:** Moderate to high, with predicted morphology of *dissociative episode* rather than depressive collapse or psychotic break. The Vazquez-arc episodes are the template; a more sustained challenge of the same type, without escape route, would produce a more sustained dissociative response, with unknown ceiling.
- **Delayed-onset symptom emergence following loss of kinetic-discharge route:** Plausible. If the portal capability were permanently disabled and the subject were held in a single reality, the predicted course would be (a) escalating irritability, (b) somatic complaints not previously seen, (c) emergence of the previously suppressed intrusion symptoms (nightmares, flashback morphology), and (d) compensatory development of either substance use or new motor-discharge behaviors. This is a testable prediction of the formulation.

---

## 4.6 Synthesis

The subject is best understood as a chronic CPTSD presentation in a body that was, by accident or design, exceptionally well-equipped to externalize the affect that the trauma generated. The kinetic-discharge architecture has been so successful that it has obscured the underlying clinical picture from the subject herself, from most of her associates, and likely from any clinician sampling her presentation briefly. The diagnosis is not subtle once the longitudinal record is integrated. What is subtle is the *prognosis*: the system is stable, the system is high-functioning, and the system is unfinished — and the conditions under which it would fail are predictable, specific, and to date have not been sustainedly imposed.

She is, in the most precise clinical phrasing available: *a trauma survivor whose survival has been so competent that the trauma has never been required to surface*. The diagnosis is correct. The treatment indication — were she ever to present for one, which the formulation itself predicts she will not — would be a long, slow, body-inclusive trauma protocol with an unusually large emphasis on tolerating stillness, conducted by a clinician with no investment in being needed and a high tolerance for being repeatedly left.


## Behavioral Atlas

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION 7: BEHAVIORAL ATLAS

## Subject: America Chavez

A longitudinal catalog of observable tells, micro-behaviors, decision habits, and condition-dependent behavioral signatures, derived from continuous-record observation across the subject's full published operational history. Organized by state. Where a behavior is multi-state, it is logged under its primary state and cross-referenced. Granularity is at the level of: posture, hand-position, vocal register, gait, eye-line, breath pattern, language choice, proxemic preference, decision latency.

---

## 7.1 BASELINE / CALM

True calm is rare in the record and is best observed in the Sotomayor University domestic intervals (*America* #2–#5), the rooftop / coffee-shop intervals with Kate Bishop (cross-record), and the post-mission decompression beats in *Young Avengers* and *West Coast Avengers*.

**Postural baseline.** Weight on the back foot, hips squared forward, shoulders dropped but not slack — a fighter's resting stance that reads as casual to civilians and as ready-to-move to anyone trained. Arms more often crossed than at sides; when uncrossed, hands are usually doing something (mug, phone, the hem of her jacket, a strand of hair pulled forward over the shoulder). She does not stand with hands hanging loose. The hanging-hands position appears to be aversive — it is the posture of waiting, and waiting is the affective category she will not occupy.

**Seated baseline.** Spreads. One leg extended, one bent; or both knees apart, elbows on knees, leaning forward. Will not sit fully back into a chair unless the chair is a couch and there is a person she trusts on it. In lecture halls (per *America* #1) she sits at the edge of the row, on the aisle seat, near an exit — a tell that holds across every interior space she occupies for more than a few minutes.

**Gait.** Long stride, slight forward lean, heels striking firmly. The walk is read by others (per multiple in-panel reactions) as a swagger; the data suggest it is partly performance and partly biomechanical efficiency — the legs are her primary weapon system and the gait keeps them loose. She does not stroll. She arrives.

**Vocal baseline.** Mid-low register, clipped consonants, declarative grammar even for non-declarative content ("we're doing this," not "should we do this"). Volume is consistently a notch above ambient — she does not have a quiet conversational mode, even at rest. Laughter is short, two-beat, often accompanied by a head-tilt back rather than a forward lean.

**Language drift.** Resting speech is English with periodic Spanish injections — endearments (*reina, mami, princesa* used both genuinely and sardonically), exclamations (*ay*, *coño*, *órale*), and structural punctuation (*claro*, *bueno*, *vale*). Frequency of code-switching tracks affect: at true calm, roughly one Spanish word per three to five sentences. Cross-reference §7.3 for elevated states.

**Eyes and gaze.** Direct eye contact, held a beat longer than American interpersonal norms — reads as confrontational to strangers, as full attention to friends. Scans rooms on entry: doors first, then high vantage points, then people. Does not scan again unless something changes. This is a threat-trained behavior that has fossilized into baseline.

**Hands.** When idle, tends to flex and unflex the fingers of the dominant hand slowly — a barely visible tic. Picks at thumbnail cuticle when seated and thinking. Does not fidget with hair, jewelry, or small objects in the way many subjects do; the hand-tells are confined to her own hands.

**Breath.** Slow, diaphragmatic, audible only on the exhale. Sighs are used as punctuation, not as distress — they close decisions ("okay" + sigh = matter settled).

**Calm-state decision habits.** Will defer low-stakes decisions to others, often theatrically ("you pick, princesa, I don't care"). Will not defer mid-or-high-stakes decisions even when not the designated leader. Latency to decision: very short. Will commit on incomplete information and adjust live rather than wait for completeness.

**Tells of true calm vs. performed calm.** True calm: shoulders drop, the back foot un-weights slightly, jaw unclenches, eyes soften at the outer corners. Performed calm (most common in team settings where she does not want to be read): identical posture but jaw is set and the breath shortens. The jaw is the most reliable single-feature tell.

---

## 7.2 LOW-GRADE STRESS / IRRITATION

Triggered by: bureaucratic environments, slow-paced meetings, indirect communication, being asked to explain herself, prolonged stillness, condescension from authority figures (especially adults toward her teen-presenting frame in early-record material), being underestimated in mixed company.

**Postural shift.** Weight redistributes evenly across both feet — she is loading. Arms cross higher on the chest, biceps engaged. The previously-relaxed jaw sets. Head tilts five to ten degrees to one side, chin slightly raised — the "really?" angle, recurrent across every artist who has rendered her.

**Vocal shift.** Volume rises a quarter-step. Sentences shorten. Sarcasm appears, dry and unsmiling. Begins to use the second person aggressively ("you want to tell me again why...") even in conversations that did not previously involve direct address.

**Language drift.** Spanish frequency increases — roughly one phrase per sentence in moderate irritation. The Spanish at this stage is *not* for warmth; it is exclusionary, used to mark the addressee as outside her circle, or to vent without translation.

**Micro-tells.** Tongue passes along the inside of the cheek (recurrent across multiple pencillers). One eyebrow lifts and stays lifted. Begins to tap a single finger — usually index — against opposite forearm while arms are crossed. The finger tap is the early warning; it appears before the subject is consciously aware of being annoyed.

**Decision habits at low stress.** Patience for process collapses first. Will cut speakers off, will summarize their argument back at them faster than they were delivering it, will pre-empt conclusions. Will offer to "just go handle it" as the resolution to almost any deliberation longer than four exchanges.

**Exit signaling.** Begins to glance toward doors / windows / open sky. In enclosed spaces will physically reorient her seat or stance to face the nearest exit. This is unconscious and predictive — by the time the glance is observable, internal departure is already underway.

---

## 7.3 ACUTE STRESS / PRE-COMBAT

Threat detected, decision imminent, body loading.

**Postural shift.** Drops into a slight crouch, knees flexing roughly fifteen degrees. Weight on the balls of the feet. Shoulders come up and forward, scapulae engaging. Hands open — fingers spread, palms loosely down at hip level. This is the launch posture and it is unmistakable; teammates who know her read it as a starting gun.

**The pre-portal tell.** Before kicking a star-portal, the subject performs a small, almost dance-like weight transfer to the non-kicking leg — a half-step back, then a hip rotation. The kicking leg lifts to roughly knee height before the launch. This is biomechanically necessary but it is also a *broadcast*: anyone who has trained with her can read the destination of a portal kick from the orientation of the hips a quarter-second before the foot connects with the air. She has never, in the record, attempted to disguise this tell — consistent with §7.1 baseline preference for declared rather than concealed action.

**Vocal pre-combat.** Drops to lower register. Switches predominantly to Spanish for the immediate pre-engagement utterance — *vámonos, ya, dale*. The pre-engagement utterance is almost always to herself, not to allies; in multi-person fights she will issue tactical English to teammates and Spanish to her own body.

**Breath.** Single deep diaphragmatic inhale through the nose, exhale through pursed lips, then breathing becomes invisible — combat breath is trained out of conscious tells.

**Eye behavior.** Pupils dilate (rendered consistently across artists in close-up panels). Eye line locks on the primary threat and does not break until the threat is neutralized; this is a vulnerability — peripheral threats have caught her in *Ultimates* and *West Coast Avengers* sequences where she had committed visual lock on a primary.

**Decision habits at acute stress.** Latency drops to near-zero. Default action: close distance and strike, or kick a portal to bring a remote threat into striking range. Will not retreat first; retreat is reserved for tactical repositioning *after* initial engagement. Will not call for backup before engaging; will call for backup mid-engagement if outmatched, and her call is a single shouted name, never a sentence.

**Tell of being genuinely outmatched.** She gets *quieter*, not louder. The swagger talk drops out. Movements become economical. This is the most dangerous version of her and the rarest in the record.

---

## 7.4 SUSTAINED THREAT / CRISIS COMMAND

Extended combat, team operations under fire, multi-front engagements.

**Leadership default.** Even on teams where she does not hold rank, sustained crisis pulls her toward the command voice — she will start issuing instructions to seniors and they will, in the record, take them. Cf. *Young Avengers*, *West Coast Avengers*, *Ultimates*. The instructions are short, imperative, and spatial ("you, left; you, up; I'm taking the portal"). She does not explain.

**Tolerance for being directed.** Limited. Will accept tactical direction from a peer she respects (Kate Bishop, late-run Hawkeye contexts; Captain America in the rare panels they share) if the direction is concrete and immediate. Will not accept direction that requires her to wait, hold position, or refrain from intervening when she sees a vulnerable party at risk — she will break formation, every time, when a non-combatant is exposed.

**Pain behavior under sustained threat.** Subject does not break stance for injuries that would drop most operators. There is a recurring micro-tell of acknowledgment — a single quick exhale, a head shake, and then resumption — that signals an injury has registered. The injury is then not mentioned. Cross-reference §2: she does not present for care.

**Communication pattern.** Comms discipline degrades under sustained engagement. She will narrate her own movement aloud, partly tactical, partly self-regulating. The narration is louder than necessary and more profane than her baseline.

---

## 7.5 INTIMACY (PLATONIC / CLOSE FRIENDSHIP)

Best-record subject: Kate Bishop. Secondary: late-run Young Avengers cohort, particularly David Alleyne and Teddy Altman in low-stakes settings.

**Proxemics.** Closes physical distance with trusted peers in a way she does not with anyone else. Will sit hip-to-hip on a couch with Kate; will hook an arm over Kate's shoulders; will put her feet in Kate's lap. The contact is consistently casual, never sexualized, and always initiated by the subject — she does not, in the record, receive uninvited touch comfortably even from close peers.

**Vocal register with intimates.** Drops a half-step lower, slows, softens at the consonants. Sarcasm becomes affectionate rather than dismissive. Spanish becomes *warm* Spanish — endearments without sardonic inflection.

**Disclosure pattern.** Will disclose facts. Will not disclose feelings about facts. ("My moms died saving a universe" — delivered as exposition, not confession.) The peers who maintain durable closeness are the ones who do not push past this line. Kate's particular value to the subject is the demonstrated, repeated refusal to push.

**Humor pattern.** With intimates, will accept being teased about her swagger, her language, her dramatic exits. Will not accept being teased about her mothers, her origin, or her competence. The boundary is unspoken and absolute; in the rare cases it has been crossed (intra-team friction in *Young Avengers*), she exits the room within ninety seconds.

**Tells of investment.** Will show up unannounced — a sign of high investment, since unannounced arrival is her preferred mode and she only deploys it where she expects welcome. Will remember small operational details about the intimate's life (Kate's apartment layout, dog's name, coffee order) and will deploy them as evidence of attention without ever naming the attention. Will bring food. Bringing food is one of the most reliable affection-tells in the record.

---

## 7.6 INTIMACY (ROMANTIC / SEXUAL)

Primary record: Lisa Halloran (*America* solo). Secondary: scattered hookup behavior, briefly indicated, in *America* and *West Coast Avengers*.

**Initiation.** Direct, unembarrassed, often verbal before physical. Will state interest in declarative form. Does not flirt by indirection; the flirt is the proposal.

**Early-relationship pattern.** Intense presence, frequent physical contact, generous attention. The subject is, in early phase, a genuinely warm partner. Tells of authenticity: relaxed jaw at rest with the partner, full reclined seating posture (the only documented context in which she fully reclines into furniture), uninterrupted sleep in the partner's presence.

**Mid-relationship inflection.** At approximately the point where the partner begins to expect availability, exit behaviors start. Tells: increased frequency of "I have to handle something" departures with vague timeframes; longer absences off-world or off-timeline framed as duty; reduced disclosure of return times; reappearance with no narrative of where she has been.

**Conflict pattern within romance.** Will not argue. Will state position, will state that she heard the partner's position, will leave the room. Returns hours or days later with no follow-up. This is the single most destructive behavioral pattern in her interpersonal repertoire and the dominant cause of the Lisa Halloran dissolution.

**Tells of impending exit (romantic).** Increased reference to off-Earth obligations. Increased pre-emptive defensiveness about her time. Reduced use of partner-specific endearments. Resumption of the §7.1 hand-flex tic during intimate conversations. Withdrawal from shared sleep — will leave the bed earlier, return later. The bed is the leading indicator.

**Post-exit pattern.** Does not initiate contact for closure. Will accept it if pushed; will not seek it. Does not, on the record, disparage former partners — neutral-to-positive references when they come up. The closed door is not bitter; it is just closed.

---

## 7.7 GRIEF

The grief record is structurally limited because the subject's defenses operate at the level of memory editing (§4) and avoidance via action (§3). What appears as grief in the panels is therefore mostly grief *signaled around the edges*, not grief expressed.

**Anniversary / reminder behavior.** When the Madres come up in conversation, the subject's tells: posture stiffens incrementally, breath shortens, eye-line drops to the middle distance rather than to the speaker. Verbal response is brief, often a single sentence, frequently in Spanish ("ellas eran todo"). She does not weep in the record on the topic of the Madres directly — once she has done so was in *Made in the USA* when the *narrative* of their sacrifice was destabilized, not the loss itself; she grieves the story more visibly than the people, which is a precise signature of memory-edited trauma.

**Grief for non-foundational losses (allies, civilians).** More accessible. Will speak briefly, will physically touch the body or the bereaved, will deliver a short statement in Spanish. Then will leave to address the cause. The action-funnel for grief is reflexive: grief becomes errand within hours.

**Tells of unmetabolized grief.** Increased Stage-2 mobility behaviors (cf. §3 stress staging). Longer absences. Increased portal use for trivial transit — she will kick a portal to go three blocks. The portal is, at this point, doing the work that crying might do in a less defended subject.

**Tells of grief reaching consciousness.** Quietness, not loudness. A half-hour of sitting still — anomalous baseline behavior, diagnostically significant. A request, rare and oblique, for company without conversation (Kate has received this; no one else in the record). A long flight, alone, at altitude, often above weather — her closest approximation of a meditative practice.

---

## 7.8 VICTORY

**Immediate post-combat.** Loud exhale, often a laugh. Will summarize the engagement in one sardonic sentence ("well, that happened"). Will check on teammates physically — eyes-on, brief contact to shoulder or arm, single question ("you good?"). Will not accept the same check returned: deflects with a joke or a shrug.

**Verbal tells of genuine triumph.** Drops into Spanish. Uses *coño* affectionately. Smiles full — the closed-mouth wry smile that is her default opens into teeth. Photographed teeth in the record are rare and almost always victory-coded.

**Decision habits post-victory.** Will refuse debrief. Will agree to celebrate, briefly. Will leave the celebration earlier than the team — typically the first to peel off. The departure is read by teams that don't know her well as dismissive; the data suggest it is a regulation strategy. Sustained group joy is, like sustained group anything, an exposure state she limits.

**The post-victory portal.** Recurrent. After a significant win, she kicks a portal and goes — sometimes to Kate, sometimes to the Utopian Parallel, sometimes to an unidentified destination. Across the record there is no observed case of her remaining with a team for the full post-victory cycle.

---

## 7.9 DEFEAT / FAILURE

**Immediate.** Goes quiet. The vocal baseline cuts out entirely for as long as several minutes. Posture: shoulders forward, hands on hips or one hand at the back of the neck. Eye-line on the ground or on the failure point itself (the fallen ally, the destroyed structure). She does not look away from the failure; she stares at it.

**Verbal pattern after defeat.** When speech resumes, it is operational and forward-pointed: "next time we — " or "we go back and — ". She will not, in the record, accept narrative framings of defeat. Will reframe to setback. The reframe is rapid and is functionally a defense; it allows the failure to be metabolized as a task rather than a loss.

**Self-blame pattern.** Internalizes failure to protect more readily than failure to win. If a civilian or vulnerable party was harmed in the engagement, the subject's tells: tightened jaw, reduced eye contact for the next several hours, sharp uptick in solo missions in the following days. She does not say *I failed*; she goes and prevents the next instance.

**Reception of comfort.** Poorly. Receives a hand on the shoulder, holds still for it, then moves. Verbal comfort produces a slight head-shake and a redirect to the next operational question. The exception is Kate, from whom comfort is received without redirect — but Kate's comfort is calibrated to her: silence-adjacent, low-affect, no demand for processing.

**The post-defeat absence.** Longer than the post-victory absence. After significant defeats (per *America* arc, *Ultimates* late-run) she will be off-grid for stretches measured in days. Returns with no narrative of where she went. This is her version of mourning the failure; it is not depression, it is decontamination through motion.

---

## 7.10 RESPONSE TO AUTHORITY

**Institutional authority (police, security, bureaucratic).** Open contempt. Will not produce ID, will not stand in lines, will physically bypass barriers. Posture goes oppositional — chin up, weight forward, arms loose. Vocal: louder, slower, deliberately provocative.

**Earned authority (peers in command, mentors who have demonstrated character).** Conditional acceptance. Will defer on terrain where the authority's competence is visible. Will not defer on terrain where her own judgment is engaged. Will signal respect through physical attention — full eye contact, body squared to the speaker — without verbal deference.

**Hostile authority (oppressors, abusers of power).** Pre-engagement protocol (§7.3) activates within seconds. The subject's most reliable trigger across the entire record is the live observation of a powerful party imposing on a vulnerable party. The interval between observation and intervention is among the shortest documented latencies in the dossier.

---

## 7.11 RESPONSE TO BEING UNDERESTIMATED

A common condition given her teen-presenting frame in early record and her gendered / racialized reception throughout.

**Tells.** Slow smile — closed-mouth, asymmetric, one corner higher. Slight head tilt. Single Spanish word, often *ay*, delivered low. Then a demonstration — almost always physical, almost always immediate. Does not argue the underestimation; corrects it by performance.

**Decision habit.** Will accept the underestimation tactically when it serves her — will let an opponent commit to a wrong assumption before correcting it kinetically. This is one of the few domains in which she displays patience.

---

## 7.12 RESPONSE TO BEING SEEN ACCURATELY

The least-documented and most diagnostically interesting state.

**Tells.** Brief freeze — half-second to one second. Eye contact breaks first, which is anomalous for her (she does not break eye contact otherwise). Hand-flex tic activates. Then one of two paths: (a) deflection by joke and topic change (the more common path) or (b) silence and a long look back at the speaker. Path (b) is rare and is observed only with Kate, in the late-run record, and with her grandmother Madrimar during the *America* arc.

**Decision habit.** Will not, in the record, engage substantively with accurate observation about her interior. Will receive it; will not respond to it. Will frequently leave the conversation within minutes — not as a fight-exit but as a regulation-exit. The accurate observation is, behaviorally, treated identically to the threat of stillness.

---

## 7.13 SLEEP, SOLITUDE, AND THE PRIVATE RECORD

**Sleep posture.** On her back, one arm overhead, the other across the stomach. Sleeps with windows open where possible. Does not sleep with the back to the door of a room.

**Private solitude behaviors (rare panels, inferred from negative space and the few depicted solo sequences).** Cooks — simply, fast, one-pan dishes that read as inherited from the Madres or the Madrimar household. Plays music aloud, frequently in Spanish, frequently loud enough that the room's other occupants would have to engage with it; the music is rarely curated for subtlety. Flies. Long high-altitude flights with no destination are her most reliable depicted solo practice and are her closest approximation of a contemplative ritual.

**The journal absence.** The subject does not journal, does not document, does not memorialize. There is no evidence in the record of any private written reflection. This is consistent with the §3 profile: introspective vocabulary undeveloped, memory editing operative, action preferred to reflection. The behavioral atlas of her interior is therefore necessarily thin — not because the interior is thin, but because the subject has organized her entire life to keep it from leaving tracks.

---

## 7.14 SUMMARY OF THE MOST RELIABLE SINGLE-FEATURE TELLS

For


## Daily Life, Routines & Rituals

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION 6: DAILY LIFE, ROUTINES & RITUALS

## Subject: America Chavez ("Miss America")

---

## 6.0 Methodological Note

A standard surveillance subject yields a week of recoverable pattern: home, transit, workplace, recurring social nodes, sleep window. The subject yields a week of *interrupted* pattern. She lives across at least three reference frames — a primary Earth-616 residence pattern, an off-world / interdimensional travel pattern, and a sporadic "drop-in" pattern with affiliated peers and teams — and her movements between them are non-Euclidean, executed by foot-portal at unpredictable intervals. What follows is the composite record built from longitudinal observation across the *Vengeance*, *Young Avengers*, *America* solo, *Made in the USA*, *West Coast Avengers*, and *Ultimates*–adjacent windows, with periodicity normalized to a representative seven-day cycle.

---

## 6.1 The Sleep Architecture

The subject is a *short, hard sleeper*. The recovered baseline is approximately five to six hours, taken in a single consolidated block beginning roughly between 01:30 and 02:30 local. She does not wind down; she switches off. Across the *America* solo record she is observed working, training, or socializing well past midnight and then asleep within minutes of horizontal — boots sometimes still on, jacket draped rather than hung, the bedside lamp left burning. The lamp-burning is a recurring datum and probably significant: the subject does not sleep in full dark.

Wake is between 06:30 and 07:30 on Earth days, earlier (by the local clock of wherever she is) when off-world. There is no observable snooze behavior. She rises in a single movement — sit, plant feet, stand — and is upright within five to ten seconds of consciousness. The first action of the day is almost invariably *movement of the body*: stretches against a doorframe, a set of pushups on a hardwood floor, a brief flight to the roof of whatever building she has slept in. Caffeine arrives second. This sequencing is invariant and diagnostic — for a CPTSD subject, the body must be confirmed *responsive* before the mind is allowed to assemble.

Naps are not observed. Sleep debt is paid in single longer blocks (eight to nine hours) every nine to twelve days, usually after a high-output combat or interdimensional sequence. She does not appear to dream eventfully — or, more precisely, no dream content is ever depicted or verbally reported, including in intimacy-adjacent depictions where it would be natural to volunteer. The absence is consistent with the §4 finding that the intrusion channel of the trauma response is suppressed.

---

## 6.2 Habitation & Habits of Place

The subject has had three documentable primary residences across the published record:

**Pre-Sotomayor (Young Avengers era).** No fixed address. The subject couch-surfs, sleeps in the Young Avengers' rotating safehouses, occasionally spends nights in pocket dimensions she has personally opened. She owns almost nothing — a duffel, a second jacket, a few books — and the lack of accumulation is a *chosen state*, not a deprivation. Every item she owns is something she can carry through a portal in a single hand.

**Sotomayor University dorm / off-campus.** During the *America* solo run she occupies a dorm room, then a small off-campus apartment. The room is sparsely furnished and *aggressively decorated* — flags (Puerto Rican, Trans Pride, the Madres' Utopian sigil), photographs taped (not framed) to the wall, a heavy-bag suspended from a structural joist she has reinforced herself, books stacked rather than shelved (Anzaldúa, bell hooks, course readers, comic anthologies — observed titles). The bed is made to a tight discipline (a tell of either military-adjacent training or institutional childhood — note for §1 / §3). The kitchen is barely used; coffee equipment is the only sustained kitchen presence.

**Post-solo / team-affiliated.** Whatever the current team's facility offers — a room in the West Coast Avengers' shared house, a bunk on the Ultimates' transit, a borrowed couch at Kate Bishop's Los Angeles apartment-office. The pattern repeats: minimal possessions, flags or fabrics on a wall, the bed tight, exits identified within hours of arrival.

**Place-habits, consistent across all three:** She sits *facing the door*, always. She stands rather than sits when conversation turns serious. She paces a defined track in any room she occupies for more than an hour — typically along the longest available wall, three to six lengths, then a stop, then continuation. She touches doorframes when passing through them — a brief two-finger contact, almost certainly unconscious, possibly a portal-readiness check, possibly a somatic grounding tic, probably both. She does not sit on beds; she sits on floors, windowsills, desks. The bed is for sleep only, an institutional-childhood signature.

---

## 6.3 The Morning Block (approx. 06:30 – 10:00)

The morning is the most regular window in the entire weekly record.

**06:30–07:00.** Wake, body-check, ten-to-twenty-minute physical set — pushups, pullups (doorframe, beam, tree branch — whatever is structural), a sequence of kicks against an imaginary or actual target. The kicks are interesting: she practices the *portal-kick* motion daily, dry, without opening anything. This is technique maintenance but also probably ritual — the body rehearses the escape it may not need.

**07:00–07:30.** Shower, brief. Hot. The subject sings or hums in the shower in Spanish — songs traceable to her grandmother's generation or to specifically Puerto Rican / Nuyorican popular music; this is one of the few unguarded vocal behaviors in the record.

**07:30–08:30.** Coffee and food. Coffee is non-negotiable, taken black, often two to three cups. Food in the morning is heavy and protein-forward — eggs, beans, leftover meat, bread — eaten standing or walking, rarely sitting. She does not cook elaborately but cooks competently; her grandmother's influence is visible in the seasoning (sofrito components, adobo, garlic-heavy).

**08:30–10:00.** This window is variable but the *function* is constant: orientation to the day's combat-or-mission situation. During the Sotomayor period this was overlaid with class attendance, badly — she would attempt the lecture, fail to remain seated, and be observed pacing the back of the room or vanishing entirely. During team periods this is a briefing or self-briefing window. During solo periods it is reading the news for things that need punching.

---

## 6.4 The Midday Block (approx. 10:00 – 16:00)

This is the *operational* window — work, training, mission execution. There is no fixed pattern beyond a fixed *intensity*. The subject does not have a job in the conventional sense; her "work" is interventional heroism, scheduled by the world's emergencies rather than her own calendar.

Within this block the surveillance record captures recurring categories of activity:

- **Training.** Heavy-bag work, sparring partners when available (Kate Bishop, the West Coast roster, occasionally Utopian Parallel warriors when she has crossed back). Sessions run forty-five to ninety minutes, no observed warmup-cooldown discipline; she enters at full intensity and stops when satisfied. Sweats heavily; does not wipe down equipment afterward — a small but consistent inconsideration.
- **Travel.** Frequent. The portal-kick is used as casually as a subway transfer; she will open a portal to cross a city if she is in a hurry, and a portal to cross a galaxy if she is not. Observed multi-leg days: Sotomayor → Utopian Parallel → Asgard-adjacent training ground → Brooklyn rooftop → Sotomayor, all inside one afternoon.
- **Combat.** When in combat: total focus, no observable hesitation, conversational only at the level of taunt or instruction. Combat is the activity in which she is most *integrated* — affect, cognition, and body collapse into a single uncomplicated channel. She is, by every behavioral metric, *happier* in combat than at rest.
- **University attendance (Sotomayor era).** Lectures: poor attendance, poor sustained presence. Seminars and discussion classes: better, when the topic is political or literary; she contributes forcefully and interrupts. Study groups: avoided. Office hours: never observed.
