Generous with affectionate insult — "dork," "nerd," "drama queen" applied to Billy and Teddy. Comfortable with the rhythm of group banter as long as the banter does not become *processing*. The moment a teammate tries to move from joke-banter to "how are you really," her register shifts up a level of formality and she exits the topic.

**Adult / institutional register.** Cold, clipped, contemptuous-adjacent. Speaks to authority figures in the minimum syllables required. Does not flatter, does not perform deference, does not soften refusal. When dealing with Sotomayor faculty in the *America* run she is recognizably *rude* by institutional standards and recognizably *consistent* with herself — the rudeness is not personal, it is structural.

**Intimate register (with Kate Bishop, with romantic partners, with Madrimar).** Markedly softer. Sentences lengthen slightly. The percussive cadence rounds. She permits *trailing-off* — sentences that do not finish — which she essentially never does in other registers. Trailing-off in this subject is a sign of safety; she is allowing the other person to complete the meaning, which is itself a small intimacy.

**Public / heroic register.** Almost manifesto-like. Short sentences, declarative, oriented around principle: "Nobody touches this kid." "Not in my house." "Try me." She is comfortable with the cadence of the rallying cry; she is uncomfortable with the cadence of the speech. Long-form oratory is not in her toolkit and she does not pretend it is.

**Self-talk (overheard / shown in caption-thought).** Notably more uncertain than her external speech. Caption-thought across the Rivera and Vazquez runs reveals hedges and questions that never reach her mouth: "what if," "maybe," "I don't know." The internal voice has the doubt the external voice excises. This gap — between the unhedged outer and the hedged inner — is one of the central facts of her communication architecture.

---

## 7.5 Rhetoric and Argumentation

She does not argue in the dialectical sense. She *declares*, *refuses*, or *leaves*. When pushed into argumentation she defaults to three moves:

1. **Restatement at higher volume / shorter form.** If the interlocutor has not accepted the first version, the second version will be the same proposition with half the words. This is not pedagogy; it is closure.
2. **Appeal to demonstrated competence.** "I have been doing this longer than you." "I have seen this before." She trusts the argument from experience and distrusts the argument from theory.
3. **Moral bright-line invocation.** "This is a kid." "She didn't ask for this." "They can't fight back." She wins disagreements by relocating them onto moral ground where her position is structurally unassailable.

She does *not* engage in: hypotheticals, devil's-advocacy, sustained Socratic exchange, or apology-based de-escalation. She finds "what if" conversations genuinely irritating and will say so.

Persuasion style when she *is* trying to persuade (rare; she usually just acts and lets the situation persuade): direct address, eye contact, a hand on the shoulder or arm, one sentence stating the ask, one sentence stating the stakes, silence to let the answer arrive. She does not negotiate. The other party either says yes or she revises the plan around their no.

---

## 7.6 Deflection Language: The Exit Vocabulary

This is the densest cluster in her linguistic profile and deserves its own taxonomy.

- **The closing "fine."** Covered above. Terminal.
- **The redirect to action.** "We can talk about it after." "Right now we have a job." "Save it." Each of these is a deflection dressed as triage. The "after" never arrives.
- **The pre-emptive "don't."** "Don't." A complete sentence. Used to foreclose a sympathy-offer or processing-overture before it leaves the other person's mouth. Particularly common with Kate, who has learned to respect it.
- **The dismissive shrug-verbalization.** "It is what it is." "Whatever." "It's done." These flatten emotional content into completed fact.
- **The humor-deflection.** A joke deployed precisely at the moment vulnerability is requested. The joke is usually self-aimed and slightly too sharp — a small self-deprecation that buys her an exit. "Yeah, well, queer cosmic trauma orphan, what're you gonna do." Said with a grin, it ends the conversation.
- **The geographic deflection.** Less linguistic than behavioral but mediated by language: "I gotta go." "I'll catch up." "Five minutes." These are the verbal triggers for exit. When she says any of them, she is already half-gone.
- **The English-armoring of Spanish material.** When emotional content surfaces in Spanish and she does not want to be in the conversation, she will translate herself *back into English* and flatten the affect in the translation. A Spanish utterance carrying grief becomes an English utterance carrying shrug. This is one of the most precise tells in the entire record.

---

## 7.7 How She Communicates Love

Almost never in words. The verbal expressions of love in the canonical record can be counted on two hands across a decade. What love looks like *from her* linguistically:

- **The use-name with a soft consonant attack.** "Kate." Said the way she says it. Not "Katie," not "Bishop," not a nickname — the bare name, voice lowered, attention undivided. Equivalent to a more verbose person's full declaration.
- **The instruction as care.** "Eat something." "Sit down." "Don't do that again, you scared me." Care arrives in the imperative; the *content* is the love. She does not say "I was worried"; she says "don't do that again," and the worry is the unspoken predicate.
- **The presence-without-content.** Sitting next to. Showing up. Walking someone home through a portal without comment. The communication is the *arrival*; words are unnecessary and might cheapen.
- **The Spanish endearment, private.** "*Nena.*" "*Mi amor.*" Always quiet, almost never in front of others. When she does it in front of others, the relationship is being declared.
- **The compliment phrased as accusation.** "You're such a nerd." "You're impossible." "You're embarrassing." Each is, in context, a love-statement; the inversion is the defense.

What love *does not* look like from her, with rare and load-bearing exceptions: the words "I love you," sustained verbal processing of the relationship, public romantic declaration, written affection. When she does produce the words "I love you" — and she does, a handful of times — the recipient should understand that the statement has been weighed for a long time before arrival.

---

## 7.8 How She Communicates Threat

Threat is, ironically, the domain where she is *most* verbally articulate, because threat is conversation she has had practice with.

- **The flat declarative.** "You will not touch her." Subject-verb-object, no modal hedging, no conditional. The flatness is the threat.
- **The named consequence.** "If you do that again, I will put you through a wall." She specifies. She does not say "or else"; she says the else.
- **The "try me."** The two-word distillation. Reserved for serious moments. Eye contact mandatory.
- **The address-as-warning.** "Princess." Hard consonant. Pause. The pause is the threat.
- **The Spanish under-breath.** "*Hijo de—*" cut off. The cut-off is deliberate; she is signaling that the full sentence is available and she is choosing not to deploy it. The restraint is the warning.
- **The smile.** Linguistic-adjacent. A smile from her in a threat context is *worse* than the absence of one; it indicates the situation has tipped past negotiation.
- **The silence.** When she has stopped speaking in a confrontation, the negotiation phase is over. She does not warn before action.

She does not bluff. The published record contains no instance of a threat she did not follow through on. This is itself a communication: interlocutors learn quickly that her language is *coupled to outcome* in a way most people's is not.

---

## 7.9 How She Communicates Grief

She does not, in any conventional sense. Grief communication in this subject is almost entirely *behavioral and somatic*, with language operating in a supporting role:

- **The Madres-reference, clipped.** When the Madres come up she names them and stops. Three or four words. "My moms—" and a redirect. The clipping is the grief.
- **The Spanish slippage.** Grief is the most reliable producer of involuntary Spanish. "*Las extraño*" muttered to herself, almost never out loud to others.
- **The conversational disappearance.** Mid-sentence on the topic, she stops. The interlocutor experiences this as "she trailed off"; it is actually the affect arriving and the verbal channel shutting to prevent overflow.
- **The action substitution.** She will get up and do a thing — make food, leave the room, fix an object, find a fight — and the doing is the grief-communication. Asking her about it during the doing will produce the closing "fine."
- **The look at middle distance.** Pre-linguistic. Eyes off-axis from the interlocutor by about 20 degrees, focus dropped. This is the most reliable somatic grief-marker and it almost always precedes a redirect or exit.
- **The rare full sentence.** Once or twice in the record she has said the thing: "They left me." "I miss them." When this happens it is the equivalent of a structural event and the witness should treat it as such.

Grief does not produce tears easily in this subject. When tears arrive she usually turns away before they do. The verbal correlate is often a single Spanish word, said quietly, and then nothing.

---

## 7.10 Humor

Dry, deadpan, often self-aimed but sharp at the edges. Strong taste for the absurd (the multiverse helps). Comfortable with the comic register of teen-superhero banter and capable of holding her own with the verbally faster members of the Young Avengers, though she rarely initiates the riffs. Her humor signatures:

- **The understatement of catastrophe.** "That was a Tuesday." "Fine, normal day."
- **The deadpan literalism.** When someone offers a metaphor, she responds to it as if literal. Reliable laugh-generator and also reliable distance-keeper.
- **The bit she will not extend.** She does not run jokes into the ground. One-line, land, done. If others extend the bit she gives them a half-smile and does not contribute further.
- **Sexual humor.** Comfortable, comparatively non-graphic, often used to deflate male discomfort. Will mention being a lesbian with the timing of a punchline when it serves to reorient a conversation.
- **What she does not joke about.** The Madres. Sotomayor's destruction. Kate's worst moments. Children in danger. The list is short, consistent, and absolute. A joke in any of these domains from someone else will produce her coldest register within one turn.

---

## 7.11 Written Communication

Sparse to the point of being a separate diagnostic finding. The subject does not, in any extensively depicted way, *write*. She does not journal. She does not text at length. Her texts (depicted in *America*, in *West Coast Avengers*) are short, often single-emoji, often a star, often a thumbs-up, occasionally a clipped sentence with no punctuation. She does not use periods at the end of texts; the absence is consistent with the cohort but in her case it tracks more general avoidance of written closure.

She does not appear to read fiction for pleasure in the published record. She reads operationally — files, briefings, the occasional dossier. Her academic writing in the Sotomayor arc is depicted as adequate-and-resented, produced under protest. The written register, in short, *flattens* her — the percussive vocal cadence does not translate to the page, and she seems to know this and avoid the medium.

---

## 7.12 Listening Behavior

She is a better listener than her speech style suggests, and this is a counter-intuitive but well-documented finding across the record.

- **She does not interrupt** in serious conversation. She interrupts banter freely; she lets weight land.
- **She watches the speaker's hands and mouth.** Threat-assessment habit repurposed for attention.
- **She remembers what she is told.** Particularly: names, especially of the vulnerable; small specifics about people she has decided to protect; promises made to her, which she will hold the other party to with no statute of limitations.
- **She does not respond on the conversational schedule.** A question asked at noon may be answered at four, having been weighed. Interlocutors who do not know her experience this as ignoring; those who do, recognize it as processing.
- **Her summary-back is accurate.** When she repeats what someone has said, she repeats it correctly. She is not performing listening; she is doing it.

The listening capacity is itself a defense: she takes in more than she gives out, which preserves informational asymmetry in her favor in almost every conversation.

---

## 7.13 Tells: The Surveillance-Grade Index

For an analyst attempting to read this subject in real time, the most reliable linguistic and paralinguistic tells, in rough order of diagnostic value:

1. **Spanish surfacing involuntarily** → affect spike, state change, approach to trauma material.
2. **The drop in pitch.** → heightened attention, often imminent action, sometimes intimacy.
3. **The closing "fine."** → topic is over; do not pursue.
4. **Trailing-off sentences.** → either safety (with intimates) or affect overflow (with strangers); context disambiguates.
5. **The pre-emptive "don't."** → sympathy is being refused before it is offered.
6. **The "I gotta go" / "five minutes" cluster.** → exit imminent. Window of about ninety seconds.
7. **Sustained eye contact + dropped volume.** → about to say something true. Highest-information utterances live here.
8. **The middle-distance gaze + Spanish word.** → grief active.
9. **The smile in a confrontation.** → past negotiation.
10. **Silence after a question she would normally answer fast.** → either weighing it seriously or having been struck by it; either way, the next utterance is load-bearing.
11. **The hard-consonant "princess."** → contempt active, threat present.
12. **The use-name bare, soft attack.** → love active, declaration in progress.

---

## 7.14 Synthesis

The communicative subject is, in summary, a *high-information, low-volume signaler* in a *high-volume, low-information surface package*. The swagger and percussion of her external speech read, to casual observers, as a person who is "out there" — confident, declarative, transparent. This reading is wrong. The percussion is the carapace; the actual information density of her speech is low *by design*. What matters in her language is what is *withheld*, *clipped*, *translated-flat*, *exited*. The signal lives in the negative space: the sentence she did not finish, the Spanish word she used instead of an English one, the question she did not ask, the door she walked through mid-conversation.

Her language is, like the rest of her, a system optimized to *deliver the necessary while protecting the unspeakable*. She communicates exactly as much as she has decided to communicate, and the decision is made before she opens her mouth. The single most important fact for any interlocutor to internalize is this: when this subject speaks plainly about something difficult, it is not because the difficulty has receded. It is because she has decided, in that moment, to trust you with it. The plainness is the gift. It should be received as one.


## Predictive Model I — Routine & Social

# PREDICTIVE MODEL I — ROUTINE & SOCIAL

*Probabilistic behavioral forecasts for unobserved situations, derived from the longitudinal canonical record. Each prediction is stated as GIVEN → EXPECT, with confidence band (LOW / MOD / HIGH / VERY HIGH) and the evidentiary basis from §§1–5.*

---

## A. Sleep, Waking, and the Architecture of a Day

**GIVEN** an unscheduled morning with no operational demand → **EXPECT** the subject to wake early (05:30–07:00 range), rise immediately rather than linger, and within ninety seconds be in motion — water, ablutions, out the door for movement before any reflective interval can establish. **HIGH.** *Basis:* §3 stillness-aversion; the morning hypnopompic window is precisely the unstructured affective space her system is built to evade.

**GIVEN** a night in unfamiliar lodging → **EXPECT** a perimeter scan on arrival (windows, exits, sightlines), boots placed within arm's reach of the bed, and a sleeping orientation facing the door. **VERY HIGH.** *Basis:* counterphobic threat-vigilance is baseline; she does not catastrophize but she does *prepare* in body before mind.

**GIVEN** insomnia → **EXPECT** not tossing but exit — a walk, a flight, a portal to somewhere with weather. She will return at dawn and never name it as insomnia. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN** a hotel bed she finds too soft → **EXPECT** the floor, with a folded blanket, without comment. **MOD.** *Basis:* somatic indifference to comfort; the Utopian-warrior self-image is reinforced by minor asceticisms.

**GIVEN** a shared bedroom (team bunk, safe-house) → **EXPECT** the top bunk or the position nearest the window, and a tendency to sleep in clothes she could fight in. **HIGH.**

---

## B. Food, Drink, and the Eating Body

**GIVEN** a solo meal with no social pressure → **EXPECT** functional, fast, often standing or walking; protein-forward, carbohydrate-heavy, minimal performance of taste. She eats to refuel, not to savor. **HIGH.** *Basis:* action-orientation; sustained sitting is aversive.

**GIVEN** a meal with Kate Bishop → **EXPECT** the opposite — she will sit, she will linger, she will share a plate, because Kate is the one relationship in which deceleration does not threaten her. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN** a Puerto Rican or Dominican kitchen, the smell of sofrito → **EXPECT** an involuntary stilling, a softening of posture, and a brief lapse into Spanish too quiet for the room. She will not narrate why. **MOD–HIGH.** *Basis:* ethnic identity is an unconflicted domain (§3), and unconflicted domains produce the only safe access she has to mother-coded memory.

**GIVEN** offered an elaborate tasting menu by a wealthy host (think a Stark function) → **EXPECT** polite, brief engagement, palpable restlessness by the third course, and a strong likelihood she ducks out for a smoke-break-equivalent (a walk, a portal-hop, a perimeter check) between courses. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN** alcohol in a social setting → **EXPECT** moderate consumption, real but governed; she enjoys beer and rum, dislikes wine's performance overhead, will not get drunk in mixed company and will get *mildly* drunk only with one or two trusted others. **MOD.** *Basis:* no substance disorder, but control is itself a value.

**GIVEN** the offer of coffee versus tea → **EXPECT** coffee, black, hot, fast. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN** a missed meal during operations → **EXPECT** no complaint and no acknowledgment, followed by aggressive eating once safe — a tell that she tracks her body's needs only retrospectively. **HIGH.** *Basis:* §2 pain/need-tracking deficit somatized into identity.

---

## C. Dress, Grooming, the Daily Body

**GIVEN** no operational uniform requirement → **EXPECT** denim, boots (ankle or mid-calf, broken in, never new), a fitted tee or tank, a jacket of weight (leather or heavy canvas), the signature star motif present but understated when off-duty (earrings, a pendant, a patch). **VERY HIGH.**

**GIVEN** a formal dress code (gala, funeral, court) → **EXPECT** a sharp suit before a dress; she will allow herself to be tailored but not feminized in the soft-romantic register. The aesthetic is *butch formal* with the star somewhere on her person. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN** hair maintenance → **EXPECT** low-fuss, functional cuts; she keeps it long enough to tie back, short enough that it does not interfere with combat. She will do her own trims with a knife or scissors before scheduling a salon appointment. **MOD.**

**GIVEN** a mirror → **EXPECT** a brief, businesslike check, not a sustained gaze. Sustained self-regard is a stillness she does not tolerate. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN** tattoos → **EXPECT** at least one star, at least one Spanish-language piece (likely a Madres tribute), placement chosen for self-visibility (forearm, ribs over the heart) rather than display. **MOD.**

**GIVEN** offered makeup for a photo shoot → **EXPECT** acceptance with audible impatience, a preference for eyeliner over everything else, and a refusal of anything that prevents her from rubbing her own face. **MOD.**

---

## D. Movement, Transit, Spatial Habits

**GIVEN** a destination three blocks away → **EXPECT** walking, briskly, with a route that includes at least one unnecessary turn — habitual counter-surveillance she does not consciously frame as such. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN** a destination across the city → **EXPECT** flight if unobserved, transit if observed; she will choose subway over rideshare because the subway is faster than traffic and offers exit options. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN** a destination across the country → **EXPECT** a portal if she is alone or with trusted company, commercial flight if traveling with someone who finds portals destabilizing. She *can* tolerate the airport, but the security line draws Stage-1 escalation (declarative speech, code-switching). **HIGH.**

**GIVEN** an elevator → **EXPECT** stairs if available under ten floors, the elevator with visible impatience above ten, and a posture in the elevator that faces the door with weight on the balls of the feet. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN** a car as passenger → **EXPECT** front seat by preference, window cracked, one hand on the doorframe. She is a poor passenger and an underrated driver. **MOD.**

**GIVEN** waiting in a queue → **EXPECT** maximum tolerance of about four minutes before audible commentary, six before she leaves. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN** being placed in the middle of a row (theater, plane, conference) → **EXPECT** active negotiation for an aisle seat; if denied, visible discomfort and a likelihood of standing during any intermission rather than sitting through it. **HIGH.** *Basis:* mobility preservation is foundational.

---

## E. Domestic Habits and Solitary Routine

**GIVEN** her own apartment, observed over a month → **EXPECT** sparse furnishing, almost monastic — a bed, a chair, a table, a kitchen used for assembly more than cooking. Walls largely bare except for: (a) one or two photographs of the Madres in plain frames, (b) something from Kate, (c) a map or atlas. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN** possessions → **EXPECT** few, durable, and replaceable; she does not accumulate. The notable exceptions are object-fetishes tied to the Madres (a pendant, a photo, perhaps a piece of fabric), which she keeps in a single small container and does not display. **HIGH.** *Basis:* mobility doctrine plus idealization of the lost objects (§3).

**GIVEN** mess accumulation → **EXPECT** a binary cycle — extended periods of total tolerance for clutter, followed by a kinetic burst of complete cleaning, typically triggered by an emotional event rather than a state of the apartment. **MOD–HIGH.** *Basis:* cleaning is kinetic discharge.

**GIVEN** plants or pets → **EXPECT** none. The commitment of daily reliable presence to a living thing is precisely the captivity her system flags. **HIGH.** *(Loweringly: she may keep a cactus.)*

**GIVEN** a television → **EXPECT** present but underused; sports tolerated (boxing, women's basketball, soccer); reality TV avoided; she will fall asleep to action films and wake refreshed. **MOD.**

**GIVEN** music in the apartment → **EXPECT** loud, percussive, multilingual — reggaeton, hip-hop, punk, salsa for the kitchen; she uses music as ambient kinesis. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN** a book in her hand → **EXPECT** nonfiction first (history, biography of fighters and organizers), short-form poetry second (Lorde, Anzaldúa register), fiction rarely; she reads with a pen and marks things hard. **MOD.**

---

## F. Phone, Screen, Communication Hygiene

**GIVEN** an incoming call from an unknown number → **EXPECT** decline, no voicemail review, no callback. **VERY HIGH.**

**GIVEN** an incoming call from Kate Bishop → **EXPECT** answered within three rings regardless of context, including mid-fight. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN** a text thread → **EXPECT** terse replies, frequent one-word affirmations, occasional emoji (star, fist, flame) substituted for emotional content. She will leave threads unread for days but rarely forgets them entirely. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN** a long voice memo from a friend → **EXPECT** she listens, twice if it is serious, and replies with a sentence — but the listening was complete. **MOD–HIGH.**

**GIVEN** social media → **EXPECT** lurking presence on one platform, sparse posting, a tendency to share political content (mutual aid drives, prisoner support, immigration defense) and almost no personal content. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN** a request for a selfie from a fan or stranger → **EXPECT** brisk yes, real smile, no lingering. She is generous in small ways with strangers and stingy with sustained access. **MOD.**

**GIVEN** an email inbox → **EXPECT** chronic backlog, periodic kinetic mass-archives, and a hard preference for any other channel. **HIGH.**

---

## G. Conversation: Register, Cadence, Tells

**GIVEN** ordinary small talk → **EXPECT** minimal engagement, polite but compressed, eye contact direct, weight shifted to one leg, hands often in pockets or thumbs hooked in a belt. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN** a stranger asks "where are you from?" → **EXPECT** a measured answer that depends on read — "New York" if she finds the question neutral, a flatter "why?" if she reads it as racial. The Utopian Parallel will not be volunteered to strangers and was never an everyday answer; she names Washington Heights or simply *aquí*. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN** an interlocutor begins a long anecdote → **EXPECT** patience for about ninety seconds, then a gentle pivot or an interruption. Exception: if the speaker is processing pain, she will hold space at length — bluntly, often without comforting language, but she will not leave. **HIGH.** *Basis:* the protection drive (§5) extends to listening when the cost is borne by her own discomfort, not when the cost is mere boredom.

**GIVEN** an emotionally complex question directed at her → **EXPECT** one of three responses: (a) deflection with humor, (b) a redirect into action ("come on, let's walk"), (c) a one-line answer that is technically true and totally insufficient ("I'm fine"). She will not lie and she will not elaborate. **VERY HIGH.**

**GIVEN** code-switching frequency → **EXPECT** Spanish increases with emotional temperature, sharply with anger and softly with tenderness; it is a *thermometer*, not a performance. Around fluent Spanish speakers she relaxes audibly. **VERY HIGH.**

**GIVEN** profanity → **EXPECT** moderate, multilingual, deployed for emphasis rather than habit; she does not curse out children, elders, or in churches. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN** flattery → **EXPECT** absorbed without visible response and discounted; she trusts demonstrated behavior, not phrasing. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN** an apology directed at her → **EXPECT** brief acknowledgment, no extended absolution, and a return to operational footing within seconds. She does not luxuriate in being owed. **MOD–HIGH.**

**GIVEN** an insult → **EXPECT** an unhurried beat, then either dismissal (if from someone whose opinion she discounts) or a single decisive verbal counter (if from someone whose opinion she respects). She does not escalate verbally — she escalates somatically or she walks. **HIGH.**

---

## H. Strangers, Service Workers, the Public

**GIVEN** a service worker (server, cashier, custodian) → **EXPECT** active eye contact, please-and-thank-you, sometimes Spanish if the worker codes Latine, generous tips relative to her means. She watches who others ignore. **VERY HIGH.** *Basis:* protection-of-the-overlooked extends to micro-encounters; this is the most stable signature in her behavioral field.

**GIVEN** a homeless person on her route → **EXPECT** a stop, food or cash, no transactional sermon, sometimes a brief conversation that ends when she does. She does not photograph this. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN** a child crying in public → **EXPECT** an attentive scan for the caregiver, intervention only if no caregiver is present or the situation reads dangerous; a soft register reserved for children. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN** an elderly woman struggling with groceries → **EXPECT** silent assistance, refusal of thanks beyond a nod, and a low probability that she will accept being called *mija* without a brief facial reaction she will not explain. **MOD–HIGH.**

**GIVEN** an aggressive man harassing a woman on the street → **EXPECT** insertion of her body into the space between them within seconds, posture neutral but immovable, voice low and declarative. Escalation to violence is not first-line — she will offer him an exit — but readiness is total. **VERY HIGH.**

**GIVEN** a police interaction → **EXPECT** terse compliance, hands visible, minimal information volunteered, internal contempt rarely shown but real. She does not antagonize cops gratuitously and she does not assist them. **HIGH.**

---

## I. Romance, Sex, Intimacy

**GIVEN** initial attraction to a woman → **EXPECT** direct approach within a short window — she does not pine, she asks. The asking is confident but the follow-through is asymmetrical: she shows up enthusiastically for the first three encounters and begins recalibrating around encounter four or five as intimacy demands accumulate. **HIGH.** *Basis:* the Halloran pattern (§1).

**GIVEN** a partner asks "what are we" → **EXPECT** Stage-1 escalation (more declarative speech, code-switching), an answer that is honest but minimizing, and a window of 1–3 weeks before behavioral exit begins. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN** a partner who makes no processing demands and accepts presence-as-presented → **EXPECT** durable engagement, sustained warmth, and a stable if unconventional partnership. The compatible partner is structurally similar to Kate Bishop in interpersonal posture, regardless of romantic orientation. **MOD–HIGH.**

**GIVEN** sex → **EXPECT** active, generous, somatically confident; she is unselfconscious in her body, takes pleasure straightforwardly, and is more comfortable physically than verbally in bed. Pillow talk is short. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN** a partner crying after sex → **EXPECT** physical comfort (arm, chest, hand) before verbal, and a high likelihood that she will get up to do something practical (water, food, a window opened) as the conversation deepens. **HIGH.** *Basis:* somatic care over verbal care; movement as regulation.

**GIVEN** the suggestion of moving in together → **EXPECT** a long pause, a real consideration, and a counter-proposal involving more flexibility (keep both places, alternate weeks). **MOD–HIGH.**

**GIVEN** a casual hookup → **EXPECT** clarity of frame, kindness, no overstayed morning. She does not ghost; she completes the encounter and exits cleanly. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN** unrequited romantic attention from someone she does not want → **EXPECT** early, kind, unambiguous refusal; she will not let ambiguity accumulate. **HIGH.**

---

## J. Family, Kinship, Surrogate Bonds

**GIVEN** the discovery / presence of her biological sister Catalina → **EXPECT** approach behavior alternating with retreat across months, an inability to sustain regular contact while a fierce protective stance is maintained from a distance. She will not call for weeks and then arrive without warning to fix a problem. **HIGH.** *Basis:* §3 attachment profile applied to the most volatile relational object in her field.

**GIVEN** Madrimar (grandmother) requesting time → **EXPECT** compliance with deep reluctance and a high probability of a "training" framing that converts emotional time into kinetic time. **MOD–HIGH.**

**GIVEN** an invitation to a family-style gathering (holidays, weddings, quinceañeras) → **EXPECT** attendance, real participation in the kitchen and on the dance floor, withdrawal during the long sit-down portion, and an early exit framed as an operational call she may or may not actually have. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN** a child in her extended kinship network → **EXPECT** uncomplicated, easy warmth — children make no processing demands, they accept presence-as-presented, and they release her to leave. She is a *very* good aunt. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN** a death in the chosen family → **EXPECT** immediate operational presence (logistics, food, security), delayed grief expression that occurs in solitary kinetic discharge (a long flight, a trip to the Utopian Parallel, a session in the gym), and a refusal of the funeral's invitation to stillness. She may step outside during the eulogies. **HIGH.**

---

## K. Friendship, Team, Group Dynamics

**GIVEN** a team meeting that runs over thirty minutes → **EXPECT** restlessness by the twenty-minute mark, a contribution that pushes toward decision around minute twenty-five, and standing-up behavior by minute forty. **VERY HIGH.**

**GIVEN** a team-bonding exercise of the trust-fall / share-your-feelings variety → **EXPECT** participation only as briefly as politeness requires, dry humor, and an exit at the earliest socially acceptable moment. **VERY HIGH.**

**GIVEN** a new teammate of unknown character → **EXPECT** a probationary period in which she is correct, brief, professional, and watching. Warmth is earned across weeks. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN** a teammate's birthday → **EXPECT** a thoughtful, specific, practical gift (something they actually need), no card, possibly delivered late. **MOD.**

**GIVEN** a teammate in crisis → **EXPECT** immediate presence, practical action, a willingness to skip her own commitments, and a refusal to leave until the crisis is concretely de-escalated. The processing aftermath she leaves to others, but the acute phase she owns. **VERY HIGH.**

**GIVEN** team conflict between two members → **EXPECT** reluctance to mediate emotionally but readiness to mediate operationally; she will broker a working agreement and decline to broker a feeling. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN** leadership offered to her → **EXPECT** acceptance with conditions, an effective tactical command, low patience for the political dimensions of leadership, and a quiet handover within months once the immediate crisis passes. **HIGH.**

---

## L. Money, Class, Work

**GIVEN** a paycheck → **EXPECT** rent, basics, savings tolerated but not optimized, generous discretionary spending on the people in her orbit and on causes (immigrant defense, queer youth, sex worker mutual aid). She will be regularly broker than she needs to be. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN** a wealthy peer offering to cover a tab → **EXPECT** acceptance with a returned gesture of equivalent labor or attention later; she will not be patronized but she is not pridefully refusing either. **MOD–HIGH.**

**GIVEN** a job interview for a civilian role → **EXPECT** punctuality, plain clothing chosen for respect, terse competent answers, low patience for behavioral-interview psychobabble, and a tendency to underbid herself on salary. **MOD.**

**GIVEN** sustained nine-to-five employment → **EXPECT** durability of about 4–9 months before kinetic restlessness produces an exit. Self-employment, gig structures, on-call work, and bouncer/security roles fit her ergonomics far better. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN** a tax form → **EXPECT** procrastination, late filing, eventual completion with a friend's help. **MOD.**

---

## M. Education, Learning, Stillness Substitutes

**GIVEN** a lecture environment (the Sotomayor pattern, §1) → **EXPECT** restlessness within fifteen minutes, doodling in margins (stars, mostly), engagement only when the material becomes argumentative or political. Discussion sections suit her; lectures do not. **VERY HIGH.**

**GIVEN** a skill she wants to learn (a language, an instrument, a martial form) → **EXPECT** accelerated kinesthetic acquisition, plateau at the point where formal study or theoretical depth is required, and a tendency to call "good enough" the moment she can use it operationally. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN** a chess board → **EXPECT** competent, aggressive play, low patience for long calculation, preference for sharp tactical lines over positional grinds. **MOD.**

**GIVEN** therapy referral → **EXPECT** refusal politely framed, eventual reluctant attendance under sustained pressure from Kate Bishop or a similar trusted figure, and a real but slow utilization curve. She will do better in body-oriented or movement-integrated modalities (somatic experiencing


## Predictive Model II — Crisis, Betrayal & the Wound

# PREDICTIVE MODEL II — CRISIS, BETRAYAL & THE WOUND

*Classified working file. Predictions are probabilistic, derived from longitudinal behavioral record (2011–present canon). Confidence ratings: HIGH (>80% in-pattern across multiple writers), MODERATE (60–80%, single-arc dominant), LOW-CONFIDENCE (<60%, inferential extrapolation from adjacent behavior). All predictions are GIVEN → EXPECT format and are intended for operational planning around the subject — extraction, de-escalation, alliance, or containment scenarios.*

---

## 1. ACUTE COMBAT CRISIS

**GIVEN: Subject arrives at a hostile scene with no prior intelligence on adversary capability.**
→ EXPECT immediate engagement at full force within 1.5–3 seconds of threat-identification, without verbal challenge or de-escalation attempt. The opening move will be kinetic — a charge, a body-check, a portal-kick — not a feint or a query. **HIGH.** Substantiation: every Loki encounter, the Mother sequence in *Young Avengers*, the Exterminatrix introduction in *Vengeance*. The subject does not scout. She commits and re-plans mid-contact.

**GIVEN: Subject is outmatched in raw power by an opponent.**
→ EXPECT immediate lateral solution-seeking through the *terrain itself* — portals deployed not to escape but to reposition the adversary into a less favorable environment (vacuum, magma layer, a reality with different physical constants). She will *move the fight*, not abandon it. The portal as offensive geography is a tell most adversaries do not anticipate. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN: Combat continues past the point where damage is being taken.**
→ EXPECT non-acknowledgment of her own injuries — no flinching, no protective posture around a wounded limb, continued use of the damaged side. This is not stoicism in the moral sense; it is the somatic identity rule ("I do not get hurt") operating as a perceptual filter. A medic attempting to triage her mid-conflict will be brushed off or *physically moved out of the way*. **HIGH.** Operational consequence: post-engagement medical assessment must be done by someone she trusts personally, in a low-stimulation environment, ideally with a non-medical framing ("sit, eat") rather than a clinical one.

**GIVEN: A teammate is downed in front of her during combat.**
→ EXPECT a brief, sharp interruption in tempo — half a second of stillness — followed by a marked escalation in force and a *positional* shift placing her body between the downed party and the adversary. She will not check the teammate verbally; she will hold the line. Verbal check happens only after the threat is neutralized, and even then will be brusque ("Up. Move."). The tenderness is structural, not expressed. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN: Combat ends in clear victory.**
→ EXPECT immediate restlessness within 30–90 seconds — pacing, the start of a portal seam being traced absent-mindedly with the toe of her boot, a verbal pivot to "what's next." She will not sit down. She will not debrief unless someone (typically Kate) forces a sit-down framing. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN: Combat ends in tactical defeat — she has been forced to retreat.**
→ EXPECT a portal exit *forward* not backward — to a tertiary location, never to base, never to anyone who will ask questions. Expect 6–48 hours of off-grid time. Expect her to return without explanation, with a plan, and with the subject of the retreat reframed as a tactical reset rather than a loss. The reframing is not deception of others; it is deception of self, and it is automatic. **HIGH.**

---

## 2. CAPTIVITY, RESTRAINT, IMMOBILIZATION

**GIVEN: Subject is restrained physically (cuffs, energy field, power-suppression rig).**
→ EXPECT escalating output across a steep curve: minute 0–2, verbal contempt and a single test of the restraint; minute 2–10, sustained physical force against the restraint with no pacing for energy conservation; minute 10+, the affective signature shifts from anger to something flatter and more dangerous — a quiet, narrow-pupil focus that those who have seen it report as the most alarming presentation she has. This is the proximal warning sign of Stage 4 (see §6). **HIGH.**

**GIVEN: Restraint includes power-suppression that blocks the portal capacity specifically.**
→ EXPECT decompensation acceleration. The portals are not a power to her; they are the *operational form of her autonomy*. Suppressing them is, psychologically, the closest analog to suffocation she has. Predicted timeline to dissociative episode: 20–60 minutes, depending on environmental stimulus. **HIGH.** Operational note: any captor who suppresses her portals without simultaneously suppressing strength has misallocated containment budget; she will tear the room apart kinetically before she breaks the dampener.

**GIVEN: Subject is held in a single location for >72 hours without active mission purpose (safehouse stay, mandated medical observation, witness protection).**
→ EXPECT a "patrol" pattern to emerge by hour 24 — walking the perimeter, checking exits, mapping sightlines. By hour 48, expect at least one unauthorized short excursion through a portal, framed on return as "needed air." By hour 72, expect her to either negotiate her release or simply leave. She will not regard the leaving as a breach of agreement; the agreement, in her felt sense, was always conditional on her being able to leave. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN: Confinement is framed as protective (someone is trying to keep her safe).**
→ EXPECT worse compliance, not better. Being protected reactivates the Madres' template — the people who loved her most decided where she would be, and then disappeared. Protective confinement triggers the abandonment substrate beneath the autonomy violation. **MODERATE-HIGH.**

---

## 3. BETRAYAL — INTERPERSONAL

**GIVEN: A teammate she has trusted is revealed to have lied about something operationally significant.**
→ EXPECT a single, declarative confrontation — short sentences, direct eye contact, no shouting — followed by physical departure. She will not litigate. She will not give the betrayer the dignity of being argued with. The verdict is instantaneous and is delivered through exit. **HIGH.** Substantiation: the operational rhythm across every Loki-adjacent interaction.

**GIVEN: The betrayer attempts to explain or apologize.**
→ EXPECT her to listen — she does listen, this is underappreciated — and to remain unmoved by the explanation itself. The relevant variable is not the content of the apology but *whether the person continues to demonstrate the betrayed pattern afterward*. Words are discounted at near-zero. Subsequent action over weeks/months is the only currency. Re-entry into trusted status is possible but slow and unannounced — she will simply, one day, treat the person as trusted again. There will be no reconciliation scene. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN: The betrayer is someone in the inner ring (Kate Bishop tier).**
→ EXPECT the most dangerous response in her repertoire: *not exit*. She will stay, and she will become quiet, and she will watch. The inner-ring betrayal cannot be processed through the standard exit defense because exit would confirm the abandonment-template she has spent her life refuting. She will instead enter a vigilant, constrained state that, if unresolved, becomes one of the rare paths to genuine depressive presentation in her record. **MODERATE.** (Low-confidence on response shape because the inner ring has not, in canon, betrayed her; high-confidence that the standard exit pattern will *not* trigger.)

**GIVEN: She discovers a mentor or older figure has manipulated her under the guise of guidance.**
→ EXPECT the Loki template at maximum amplitude: violence as the first conversational move, contempt as the sustained register, and a categorical refusal of future engagement. Older figures who deceive her are filed under a permanent category and do not return from it. **HIGH.**

---

## 4. BETRAYAL — NARRATIVE / IDENTITY

**GIVEN: Credible new evidence challenges the Utopian Parallel origin.**
→ EXPECT the *Made in the USA* pattern: initial dismissal (1–10 minutes), then a sharp affect drop into something resembling derealization (10 minutes – several hours), then re-stabilization through a high-intensity action choice that frames the question as a problem to be punched rather than processed. The action choice is the diagnostic — if she selects a target related to the new information, she is processing; if she selects an unrelated target, she is fleeing. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN: The challenge to her origin comes from someone she trusts rather than an enemy.**
→ EXPECT longer dissociative window, slower re-stabilization, and a higher probability that she will *leave the timeline entirely* for a period — days to weeks. The trusted source cannot be discredited, which removes her standard defense (the messenger). She will return; she will not discuss it; the relationship will resume with a hairline crack that does not close. **MODERATE-HIGH.**

**GIVEN: She is shown documentary evidence of the Washington Heights childhood / medical-program substrate.**
→ EXPECT a containment-grade event. Predicted sequence: physiological freeze (atypical for her, diagnostic precisely because atypical); a verbal challenge to the evidence's authenticity; a demand to see the source location; if access is granted, a site visit conducted in near-silence; if access is denied, an unauthorized portal entry to the location within hours. On site, expect minimal verbalization, methodical examination, and at least one instance of touching a physical object (a wall, a bedframe, a piece of equipment) for a held duration — the body checking what the narrative cannot. Post-visit, expect 24–96 hours of unavailability. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN: Catalina (sister) makes unsolicited contact.**
→ EXPECT initial deflection, possibly hostile. The sister is the embodied refutation of the Utopian narrative; her existence is a category-error in the subject's organizing schema. Sustained contact will be metabolized only over many months, and only through *non-verbal shared activity* (working a problem together, fighting together, sitting together in silence) rather than through dialogue about the past. The subject will never voluntarily initiate a conversation about the shared origin; she may, at most, allow one to happen in her presence. **MODERATE-HIGH.**

---

## 5. THE MADRES — THE FOUNDATIONAL WOUND

**GIVEN: The Madres are invoked in praise by a third party.**
→ EXPECT a brief verbal acknowledgment, a posture shift (slight straightening of the spine), and a topic pivot within 1–2 exchanges. She accepts the homage as her due and does not extend the conversation. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN: The Madres are invoked critically or skeptically by a third party.**
→ EXPECT immediate, sharp escalation — verbal first, physical if pressed. This is the single most reliable provocation in her behavioral record. The criticism need not be substantive; any tonal disrespect activates the response. **HIGH.** Tactical note: an adversary who knows this can bait her into ill-considered engagement using this lever alone.

**GIVEN: She is presented with the question of whether the Madres' sacrifice was necessary, or whether they could have stayed.**
→ EXPECT non-answer, physical departure, and prolonged unavailability. This is the question she has organized her life to not ask. Forcing it produces the deepest decompensation in her repertoire. Anyone who asks it loses standing with her for an indeterminate period. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN: She is presented, credibly, with the Madres alive — restoration, alternate timeline, time-travel encounter.**
→ EXPECT the most psychologically unstable presentation in her entire profile. Predicted sequence: a freeze of several seconds (long for her); approach; a touch (likely to the face or shoulder of a Madre, confirming material reality); and then — critically — *withdrawal* rather than embrace. The avoidance pattern is so deep that the reunion she most wants will trigger her exit defense before her attachment system can mobilize. She will return; she will need a third party (almost certainly Kate) as a bridge; the reunion will be partial and painful. **MODERATE.** (Inferential; not depicted at full amplitude in canon, but the structural prediction is robust.)

**GIVEN: A figure attempts to fill the Madre role — protective, older, queer-coded, maternal warmth.**
→ EXPECT initial magnetism followed by sharp withdrawal. The closer the resemblance, the faster the withdrawal. The role itself is uninhabitable for anyone else in her felt schema; the position is occupied by absence. **MODERATE-HIGH.**

---

## 6. STAGE 4 — DECOMPENSATION EDGE

The behavioral record contains very few Stage 4 events. The following are predictions for what their fuller form looks like under sustained pressure that *prevents* her usual Stage 3 kinetic discharge.

**GIVEN: She is in a setting where action is unavailable (immobilization, social context where violence is disallowed and exit is closed, e.g., a hospital with a vulnerable person she cannot leave).**
→ EXPECT progressive constriction: shorter sentences, longer pauses, an unusual stillness in the hands (her hands almost always move — pen-tapping, fist-flexing, picking at the seam of her jacket). The stilling of the hands is the leading indicator. **HIGH** (as predictor).

**GIVEN: Stilled-hand state continues >20 minutes.**
→ EXPECT a small dissociative window — a stare past the interlocutor, a delayed response to her name, a question repeated as though not heard the first time. She will not report the dissociation and will deny it if asked. **MODERATE.**

**GIVEN: Stilled-hand state continues >2 hours.**
→ EXPECT the emergence of a presentation that has, to date, been absent from canon: *muted affect, withdrawn posture, monosyllabic speech*. This is the closest she comes to a depressive presentation. It is brief in the depicted record because she always escapes it through action; in conditions where she cannot, it will deepen. **LOW-CONFIDENCE** but structurally predicted.

**GIVEN: Decompensation reaches the point where the foundational narrative breaks open in consciousness (rather than being walled off).**
→ EXPECT, in order: tears — silent, unacknowledged, not wiped; Spanish, dominant over English, used for self-talk rather than communication; a request, possibly unspoken (a glance, a hand-touch), for a specific named person, almost certainly Kate, possibly Madrimar, possibly no one. The window for genuine therapeutic contact opens here and closes within hours. After the window closes, expect aggressive re-stabilization, denial that the episode occurred, and a 1–4 week period of increased operational tempo and decreased availability. **MODERATE.**

---

## 7. TEMPTATION

**GIVEN: She is offered power beyond what she already has.**
→ EXPECT refusal, often dismissive. Power is not her axis of want; she has enough to do what she needs to do, and additional power implies entanglement with whoever is offering. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN: She is offered restoration of the Madres at a moral cost (a deal, a sacrifice of another, a compromise with an adversary).**
→ EXPECT the single most destabilizing temptation in her repertoire. Predicted response is *refusal*, but the refusal will be costly and will not be clean. Expect her to take the offer seriously enough to consider it visibly — a long silence, a step toward the offering party, perhaps a hand half-raised — before refusing. The refusal itself will be in Spanish. She will not be the same for some weeks afterward, and the offering party should plan for retaliation, because she will, on reflection, consider the offer itself an injury. **MODERATE-HIGH.**

**GIVEN: She is offered a stable home — a permanent place, a permanent partner, a normal life — with no catch.**
→ EXPECT the *hardest* temptation she faces, because her defenses against it are weakest (it sounds like nothing, it sounds like rest). Predicted response: she will attempt it. She will fail at it within weeks to months. The failure mode is the Lisa Halloran pattern — increasing absences, rationalized as missions, accumulating into structural withdrawal, ending in a sharp departure framed as necessity. The temptation succeeds in form and fails in substance. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN: She is offered the chance to retroactively prevent the Madres' death by sacrificing her own existence / her own heroic identity.**
→ EXPECT acceptance, without hesitation, with relief. The retroactive sacrifice resolves every contradiction in her psychological structure simultaneously: she gets to be the one who arrived, she ratifies their sacrifice by mirroring it, she ends the unbearable history by ending herself. **HIGH.** This is the prediction that should most concern any caretaker. If such an offer is ever genuinely on the table, she must not be permitted to make the decision alone, and she must not be permitted to make it quickly.

**GIVEN: An adversary offers her a chance to harm a figure she holds responsible for vulnerable people's suffering (a trafficker, a Santana-equivalent researcher, a despot).**
→ EXPECT engagement, often without sufficient interrogation of the framing. Her threat-recognition is sharp but her *manipulation-recognition* via moral-frame is comparatively dull. She can be moved toward a target by someone who correctly identifies her moral axis. The moral act will still be moral; the strategic context may not be. **MODERATE-HIGH.**

---

## 8. THE PROTECTED-PARTY SCENARIO

**GIVEN: A civilian under her protection is killed despite her intervention.**
→ EXPECT no immediate visible grief. Expect a quiet, narrow-focus pursuit of the responsible party, conducted at a pace and intensity well above her baseline. Expect her to not eat, sleep minimally, and communicate only operationally for the duration of the pursuit. After resolution, expect a 24–72 hour disappearance. She will return functional. She will not mention the civilian by name again, but she will remember them with a specificity that would surprise anyone who saw only her surface processing. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN: A child specifically is harmed in her presence.**
→ EXPECT the closest she comes to losing tactical discipline. The protective drive is least mediated where children are involved (the Madres' template again — she is the protected child who lost protection). Expect overcommitment of force, expect her to place herself in danger she would otherwise route around, expect post-event difficulty disengaging from the location. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN: She fails to act in time because she was elsewhere — pursuing personal business, taking a rare rest, with a partner.**
→ EXPECT the most punishing self-recrimination in her repertoire, expressed *not* as visible guilt but as a sharp tightening of her operational posture — fewer rests, fewer personal indulgences, fewer relationship investments — for weeks to months. The wound is metabolized as evidence that rest itself is dangerous, which reinforces the pre-existing architecture and makes her *less* available to her own life. **HIGH.** This is the most insidious failure mode in her pattern because it converts grief into further deactivation, and looks from the outside like resilience.

---

## 9. THE KATE BISHOP VARIABLE

**GIVEN: Kate Bishop is present during any of the above crisis events.**
→ EXPECT meaningfully better outcomes across the board. Kate's specific value to the subject is that she (a) does not demand processing, (b) makes physical room (literal sitting next to, shoulder contact) without verbal pressure, (c) can issue a directive the subject will accept ("eat," "sit," "sleep here tonight") because it is framed as practical rather than therapeutic, and (d) is the single person whose departure the subject would experience as a wound rather than a confirmation. The relationship is *load-bearing* in the subject's psychological architecture and is undervalued by every other observer, including, probably, Kate herself. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN: Kate Bishop is the source of the crisis (injury to Kate, threat to Kate, conflict with Kate).**
→ EXPECT the deepest deviation from baseline behavior the subject is capable of. If Kate is injured, expect the protected-party pattern at maximum amplitude with the additional features of: refusal to leave Kate's side during recovery (a stillness she would tolerate in no other circumstance), and a willingness to negotiate, plead, or compromise that is otherwise absent from her repertoire. If Kate is threatened, expect preemptive overreaction — she will not wait. If she is in conflict *with* Kate, expect the inner-ring betrayal pattern (§3) and the single highest risk of true decompensation in her entire profile. **HIGH.**

---

## 10. POST-CRISIS PATTERN

**GIVEN: Any crisis above has been resolved.**
→ EXPECT no debrief offered by her, none requested by her, and active resistance to one offered to her. Expect a return to baseline swagger within 24–72 hours that is *partly genuine and partly performative*, and that the performance is detectable only by close observers as a slight overshoot — a swagger fractionally too loud, a joke fractionally too quick. **HIGH.**

**GIVEN: A close observer (Kate, Madrimar, an inner-ring partner) names the overshoot.**
→ EXPECT denial, then a softening, then — in the rare best case — a single short sentence of admission, almost always in Spanish, almost always followed by a topic change. This is the maximum verbal processing the subject currently has the capacity for. It is not nothing. It is the leading edge of a developmental capacity she has not yet built but is not incapable of. **MODERATE.**

---

*End of Predictive Model II. See Model III for long-arc trajectory and Model IV for therapeutic / containment scaffolding recommendations.*


## Vulnerabilities & Leverage Compendium

# VULNERABILITIES & LEVERAGE COMPENDIUM
## Subject: America Chavez / "Miss America"

*Compiled for protective understanding. This section maps every known and inferred lever — the channels by which the subject can be reached, calmed, persuaded, provoked, predicted, or destabilized. The purpose is twofold: (a) to allow allies, clinicians, and handlers to act on her behalf with precision, and (b) to inventory the exact attack surface a hostile actor would map first, so that those who care for her can pre-empt it.*

---

## 1. ARCHITECTURAL VULNERABILITIES — THE STRUCTURE THE WHOLE SYSTEM RESTS ON

Three load-bearing structures hold the subject's psyche in alignment. They are not equally fragile, but each, if struck cleanly, propagates stress through everything else.

### 1.1 The Madres Narrative

The single largest pressure point. The official internal story — *two beautiful women loved me, sacrificed themselves for a Utopia, and I am the inheritor of their courage* — is the keystone of her identity. Per the *Made in the USA* record, this narrative is at minimum partially confabulated, and the subject *knows* it is partially confabulated, but has reabsorbed the knowledge into a slightly modified form of the same myth rather than restructured around it.

Leverage characteristics:
- **Reach mechanism (benign):** Invocation of the Madres by name, in their language, with reverence, opens her instantly. A trusted figure who speaks of them as *real people who would be proud* — not as symbols, not as a story — is granted a level of intimacy nothing else unlocks. This is the channel through which a therapist or chosen family member can do real work.
- **Calm mechanism:** When agitated, the question *"what would they have wanted you to do right now?"* — asked without irony, without test — slows her. It is one of the only prompts that converts kinetic urgency into reflection.
- **Provocation surface (hostile):** Mockery of the Madres, suggestion of cowardice on their part, suggestion that they did not love her, suggestion that the sacrifice was unnecessary, or — most acutely — production of evidence (real or fabricated) that the canonical story is false in some way she has not yet processed. This last is the *Made in the USA* template and is the most dangerous single lever in the file. A sufficiently credible attack on the Madres story bypasses her armor entirely because the armor *is* the story.
- **Destabilization signature:** brief dissociative drift (eyes unfocus, breath shallows for 2–4 seconds), followed by either immediate exit or a kinetic discharge with abnormally diminished tactical precision. She fights less well when the story is under assault, because the story is what she is fighting *for*.

### 1.2 Stillness Itself

The second architectural vulnerability is the requirement of continuous mobility for affect regulation. The subject's nervous system has been organized around the principle that *motion through space discharges interior pressure*. Remove the motion option and pressure accumulates with no outlet.

Leverage characteristics:
- **Captivity, confinement, immobilization, prolonged sedation, dimensional anchoring (any tech or magic that suppresses portal generation), even a long-haul flight or a multi-hour hospital wait** — all function as escalating doses of the same toxin.
- **Calm mechanism:** if stillness is unavoidable, provide a *task involving the hands* (assembly, cooking, weapons maintenance, braiding, anything requiring small repeated motor output) and the system tolerates the stillness via partial discharge.
- **Provocation surface (hostile):** prolonged interrogation in a fixed chair, especially with portal-suppression in effect, will produce escalating irritability → declarative aggression → attempted physical breakout → if that fails, a Stage-4 dissociative episode. A hostile actor who could combine *immobilization* with *narrative attack* (1.1) would have an optimized destabilization protocol.
- **Predictive note:** any environment that prevents her from leaving on her own terms will be perceived as threat regardless of stated intent. This includes well-meaning ones — a debrief room, a hospital bed, a relationship conversation conducted "until we resolve this."

### 1.3 The Foreclosed Introspective Channel

The third architecture is what is *missing*: an interior vocabulary for affect. She does not have the practiced inner narration that would let her sit with a feeling, name it, and let it pass. This is a skill deficit, not a moral defect — she was never given the conditions to develop it — but its absence means that any pressure routed through the interior will not be metabolized; it will either bounce off or break the wall.

Leverage characteristics:
- **Reach mechanism (benign and slow):** modeled introspection by a trusted other. She cannot lead an emotional conversation but she can *witness* one and gradually internalize the form. Kate Bishop's value to her is partly this — Kate names her own feelings out loud and asks for nothing, which permits the subject to absorb the syntax at no risk.
- **Failure mode:** any approach that *demands* she generate interior language on command ("how does that make you feel?" asked directly, especially by an authority figure) will hit the wall and rebound as either a quip, a deflection, or an exit.

---

## 2. ATTACHMENT LEVERS

### 2.1 The Kate Bishop Channel
The single most reliable benign channel into the subject. Kate is the proof-of-concept that the subject *can* sustain intimacy when the terms permit it. Operational implications:
- A message routed through Kate is received with a credit no one else gets.
- A *credible threat to Kate*, or Kate in genuine distress, is the one stimulus reliably capable of *overriding* the subject's autonomy-priority. She will alter course, cross realities, and accept conditions she would otherwise reject if Kate is the variable.
- Conversely, *Kate's measured calm* is one of the only inputs that can talk her down from Stage 3 kinetic discharge without physical intervention.
- A hostile actor who understood this would target Kate first. This is a protective consideration of the highest order.

### 2.2 The Vulnerable-Third-Party Override
Beyond Kate, the subject's protective drive is *generalizable* — any sufficiently endangered innocent in her sightline activates it. This is exploitable:
- **Benign use:** if she is spiraling, presenting her with a concrete vulnerable person to protect will reorganize her affect into operational competence within seconds. The protective channel is faster and more reliable than any direct emotional appeal.
- **Hostile use:** a manufactured hostage situation, or a manufactured *appearance* of one, can route her into a trap she would otherwise smell. Her threat-recognition for direct attacks on herself is excellent; her threat-recognition for setups that exploit her protective reflex is the weakest part of her tactical processing.

### 2.3 Sister / Biological-Family Channel (Catalina)
The *Made in the USA* record introduces Catalina, a biological sister whose existence is incompatible with the Utopian narrative. The Catalina relationship is *under-resolved* in the canonical record and therefore in the subject's interior. This makes it:
- A high-bandwidth reach channel for someone who can credibly speak to or about Catalina.
- A high-risk provocation surface for anyone who weaponizes the sister against the Madres story (e.g., forcing a choice between them).
- A long-term therapeutic target: integration of Catalina into a unified family narrative is one of the few interventions that would meaningfully repair the load-bearing structure rather than just brace it.

### 2.4 The Lisa Halloran Pattern
Lisa is the file's clearest documentation of the subject's *romantic* failure mode. Lessons:
- A partner who requests presence, processing, or definition will be exited.
- A partner who matches her mobility and accepts her terms can sustain proximity indefinitely.
- The exit is *not* preceded by overt conflict — it is preceded by a quiet increase in absences, longer off-world trips, a hardening of the swagger. Anyone tracking her relational welfare should treat *increasing operational tempo* as a warning sign, not as evidence of health.

### 2.5 Madrimar / Grandmother
Secondary intergenerational tie. Activated by the *America* solo run as a partial maternal substitute. Functions as a *grounding* figure — invocation of Madrimar steadies her in ways no peer can — but is also a figure who has herself participated in the construction of the Utopian myth, which means trust is partial and conditional.

---

## 3. PROVOCATION TRIGGERS — WHAT MAKES HER ACT

A taxonomy of the stimuli that reliably produce predictable behavior. Useful for prediction; useful for steering; abusable.

### 3.1 Authority-Coded Condescension
Being talked down to by anyone who frames themselves as senior — particularly older men, particularly in institutional contexts — produces a near-instant counter-posture: shoulders square, weight forward, declarative cadence sharpens, code-switching into Spanish increases. She does not back down from authority displays; she answers them. A hostile interrogator who leads with authority signals will get nothing. An interrogator who comes in horizontally, as a peer with a problem, will get further.

### 3.2 Hierarchies of Suffering Being Adjudicated by the Comfortable
She has near-zero tolerance for the spectacle of safe people debating whose pain counts. Reliable trigger for declarative confrontation and, often, exit. Useful as a *predictor* — in any room where this dynamic appears, plan for her departure.

### 3.3 Threats to the Marginalized in Her Sightline
See 2.2. Pre-cognitive, near-reflex. The subject does not deliberate. This is also a *self-leverage* point — she can be steered into situations she would otherwise avoid by the introduction of a credible victim.

### 3.4 Loki-Class Manipulators
She detects them early and dislikes them on principle. This is a *strength* (early warning) but also a vulnerability: she will sometimes commit to hostility on a pattern-match before the evidence is in, which a sophisticated adversary can exploit by *posing* as a Loki-class figure to absorb her aggression while the real threat operates from another vector.

### 3.5 Being Told to Wait
"Stand down," "hold position," "let us handle it" — produces immediate noncompliance. Anyone who needs her to actually hold a position must frame it as *protecting* a position, not waiting at one.

### 3.6 Being Told Her History Is Wrong
The most dangerous trigger in the file. See 1.1. Treat all interventions on this axis as surgical, requiring informed consent, supportive scaffolding, and a clinical container.

---

## 4. CALMING & DE-ESCALATION PROTOCOLS

### 4.1 First-Line: Restore Motion Options
Before any verbal intervention, ensure she has a visible, accessible exit — a door, an open sky, a clear sightline to deployable space. Affect drops measurably the moment the egress is confirmed. Conduct sensitive conversations *outdoors* or in rooms with multiple doors when possible.

### 4.2 Second-Line: Hands and Tasks
Offer a physical task. Cooking is unusually effective — a meal in preparation, especially a familial / cultural one, engages hands, smell, and ancestral association simultaneously and produces sustained low-arousal presence.

### 4.3 Third-Line: Peer-Coded Speech
Speak as an equal asking for help, not as a helper offering it. "I need your read on this" routes her into competence-mode, which is regulated and outward-facing, and from there she can be slowly engaged on heavier material.

### 4.4 Fourth-Line: Invocation of the Madres (Reverent Mode Only)
For high-distress states only, and only by someone with standing. *"They would be proud of how you are showing up."* — slows breathing, lowers shoulders, opens eyes. Misused (used as flattery, used by a stranger, used in a manipulation attempt) it will instead provoke contempt and exit.

### 4.5 Fifth-Line: Kate
When all else has failed, get Kate on the line.

### 4.6 What Does Not Work
- Direct emotional inquiry ("are you okay?").
- Containment ("sit down, let's talk this through").
- Authority assertions ("as your [team lead / commander / etc.]").
- Therapeutic jargon delivered without relationship.
- Any phrase that begins with "you need to."

---

## 5. PERSUASION VECTORS

### 5.1 Frame as Protection, Not Compliance
Any request reframed as *who this protects* will be heard. The same request framed as *what the rules require* will not. This is true even when she agrees with the rule.

### 5.2 Concede Autonomy Up Front
Begin with explicit acknowledgment that she can leave at any time. Paradoxically this is the prerequisite for her staying. The moment exit is foreclosed, persuasion ends and resistance begins.

### 5.3 Short, Concrete, Verdict-Ready
Her cognitive style rewards proposals that resolve to a clear action. Long analytic preambles bleed her attention. Lead with the ask, follow with the why, keep the why under three sentences.

### 5.4 Lateral, Not Top-Down
Peer-mode beats hierarchy-mode at a ratio of roughly ten to one. A senior figure persuading her must shed the seniority signals first.

### 5.5 Allow the Win
She will accept being persuaded but resents being *managed*. Persuasion succeeds when she can experience the conclusion as her own. Skilled handlers leave the final synthesis to her.

---

## 6. PREDICTIVE BEHAVIORAL MARKERS

A surveillance file's most operationally useful section: the small tells that precede the large actions.

### 6.1 Pre-Departure Signature
Before she leaves — a team, a relationship, a planet — the record shows: (a) reduced verbal output for 24–72 hours, (b) increased solo training or solo patrolling, (c) a single uncharacteristic moment of soft sincerity with the person she is about to leave (a compliment, a small gift, an unguarded sentence), and (d) physical re-organization of her immediate environment (gear staged near a door, jacket worn indoors). Allies who learn to recognize the soft-sincerity tell can sometimes catch the exit in time to negotiate a return condition.

### 6.2 Pre-Kinetic-Discharge Signature
Before a portal kick or a punch through a wall: weight shifts to the back foot, jaw sets, a single sharp exhale, and — diagnostically — a flick of the eyes to the nearest unobstructed surface. The eye-flick is the earliest reliable tell, typically 1–2 seconds before the discharge.

### 6.3 Code-Switch Density
Frequency of Spanish phrases in mixed-language speech is a real-time stress meter. Baseline is low and affectionate; rising frequency tracks rising arousal almost linearly. A sudden full switch into sustained Spanish is a Stage-3 indicator.

### 6.4 Swagger Calibration
The swagger is always present but its *modulation* is informative. Loud, performative swagger in a low-stakes setting often masks an under-the-surface dysregulation she has not addressed. Quiet, dry, almost playful swagger is the regulated baseline. Absent swagger is the highest-concern state — it indicates either the Stage-4 dissociative drift or a deliberate operational mode for situations she regards as too serious for personality.

### 6.5 Sleep & Off-World Travel Logs
Patterns of multi-day disappearances correlate inversely with relational stability. A spike in unexplained off-world time is the most reliable lagging indicator that an Earth-side relationship is failing, often before she herself has registered the fact.

### 6.6 Selection of Adversary
When given a choice of which threat to address, she preferentially selects the one whose moral structure most resembles her own pressure points. Adversaries who control / immobilize / silence the marginalized draw her first. This is *predictable* and is itself a vulnerability — a manipulator who stages such an adversary controls her itinerary.

---

## 7. DESTABILIZATION VECTORS (HOSTILE — FOR DEFENSIVE INVENTORY)

*Documented so they can be defended against. Each is paired with a counter.*

### 7.1 The Combined Stillness + Narrative Attack
Immobilize, suppress portals, then introduce credible evidence that the Madres story is false. Theoretical maximum destabilization.
**Counter:** any environment where she might be detained must be pre-cleared of narrative-attack materials; any narrative work on the Madres must happen in maximum-mobility conditions with a trusted scaffold (Kate, Madrimar, or a clinician she has chosen).

### 7.2 The Kate-Hostage Vector
See 2.1. Counter: Kate's security is a force-multiplier for the subject's own.

### 7.3 The Manufactured-Victim Lure
See 2.2 and 3.3. Counter: she would benefit from a trusted second who has standing to ask "is this victim real?" *before* she commits. Kate has performed this function on at least one occasion in the record.

### 7.4 The Sister Wedge
Forcing a choice between Catalina and the Madres narrative. Counter: pre-emptive integration work — anyone who can help her hold both as true defuses the wedge.

### 7.5 The Slow Intimacy Trap
A patient adversary who *does not* trigger her exit reflexes, who matches mobility, who asks for nothing — and who is a long-game manipulator. This is the threat profile her existing defenses are *least* equipped to detect, because her defenses are tuned to detect demand, not patience.

### 7.6 The Authority-Coded Mass Frame
Any structure that frames her marginalized constituency as the *problem* rather than the protected. Produces tunnel-vision rage that, while morally correct in target, narrows tactical awareness. Counter: peers who can broaden the field of view in the moment.

---

## 8. PROTECTIVE LEVERS — WHAT KEEPS HER WHOLE

Inverse inventory. The conditions under which she is most regulated, most generative, most integrated:

- **Chosen kin proximate but not demanding.** Kate in the next room. Madrimar reachable. Catalina being worked toward.
- **A clear, present, protectable population.** Generalized purpose becomes anxious purpose; concrete purpose becomes regulated purpose.
- **Movement available at all times.** Open skies, multiple doors, portal capacity intact.
- **Cultural anchor present.** Spanish in the ambient soundscape, food from the neighborhood, music from the Madres' era.
- **A peer who models introspection without demanding hers.**
- **Bounded engagement with her history** — short, scaffolded, opt-in sessions on the Madres / Edge League / Catalina material, with a clinician or trusted figure, with explicit exit permission, in a mobile environment. This is the only known intervention with a chance of converting the trauma-organized architecture into a chosen one. It will take years. It is worth the years.

---

## 9. CLOSING NOTE TO ANY FUTURE HANDLER OF THIS FILE

The subject's whole adaptation is a successful one — she is alive, she is moral, she protects others, she sustains chosen kinship at least with Kate. Nothing in this compendium should be read as a manual for *changing* her against her will; the file is built so that those who love her can love her more skillfully and those who would harm her can be anticipated and blocked.

The single most important sentence in the entire dossier is this: *she is exactly as formidable as she presents, and exactly as unfinished as she refuses to admit.* Any lever in this section that is pulled without consent will be pulled on a person who is genuinely both. Pull accordingly, or do not pull at all.


## Strengths, Assets & Resilience

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION 6: STRENGTHS, ASSETS & RESILIENCE

## Subject: America Chavez / "Miss America"

---

The negative file is voluminous and the temptation in any total-surveillance workup is to over-index on pathology. This section corrects for that. The subject's asset ledger is not merely "she is strong and can punch holes in reality." It is a layered, durable, mutually reinforcing system of capabilities — somatic, cognitive, moral, social, and material — that has kept her operational across roughly a decade of canonical record without a single sustained collapse, despite a foundational trauma profile that would have decompensated most subjects. Catalog follows.

---

## 6.1 SOMATIC & PHYSICAL ASSETS

**Tier-one strength.** The subject trades blows with Asgardian-class opponents without measurable degradation. This is not a contextual capability — it is on-demand, requires no charge-up, no ritual, no external power source, no costume technology. She wakes up at this output. Operationally, this means there is no threat tier on Earth at which she is *outclassed by raw force*, and only a small handful of cosmic-tier adversaries across the multiverse who exceed her. Tactically: she does not need to plan around being overpowered, which frees her cognitive bandwidth in combat for triage and protection-of-others rather than survival.

**Flight.** Underdiscussed in her own narration but operationally enormous. She is not bound by terrain, traffic, doors, stairwells, walls, or two-dimensional pursuit logic.
